Anhui Finance Director Ye Yuanlong Goes to Beijing

(Anqing) Ye Yuanlong, Director of the Department of Finance,

Anniversary of the September 18th Incident 9

Today marks the first anniversary of the tragic September 18th Incident in our Northeast. How should we, as a people, spend this anniversary? Has our domestic situation seen any changes in this year? Today, instead of stamping our feet and wringing our hands, pouring out our hearts and minds in passive commemoration, how about calming our minds and silently reflecting on the events of this past year, making a thorough reckoning, and thereby seeking a path forward for our future efforts?

From September 18th of last year to September 18th of this year, this year is truly the most humiliating and unbearable year for our nation. If we speak of "lying on firewood and tasting gall," then this year should be the time for our nation to lie on firewood and taste gall. If we speak of "wiping out shame and striving for strength," then this year should also be the beginning for our nation to rise with determination. However, after a year, the serious situation in diplomacy has not shown any signs of easing, and the state of disunity within our country seems to have worsened. The great stimulus of the September 18th Incident and the countless wounds in this year seem to have no reaction in our nation. How to save the national crisis remains as it was, untouched. This is what makes us the most grieved and helpless.

The Hei River sobs, the Bai Mountains darken. We look out at the shattered mountains and rivers of the Northeast. The tragic scene of the September 18th Incident last year is truly unbearable to recall, but how can we forget it for a moment? Let us now try to silently review this bloody account from the beginning.

On the night of September 18th last year, the Japanese army suddenly launched a forceful attack, occupying our Shenyang, a tragic incident unprecedented. The occupation of Shenyang became the start. After Shenyang was occupied, they immediately attacked important cities along the South Manchurian Railway, such as Changchun, Andong, and Yingkou. Overnight, all fell into the hands of the Japanese. On the 21st, they attacked Jilin City, further west to Zhengjiatun and Tongliao. In less than a week, the Japanese army had already occupied most of our Liaoning and Jilin provinces. At the end of October, the Japanese army attacked Qiqihar again. Although the troops under Ma Zhanshan resisted fiercely, Qiqihar was captured on November 18th. In December, the Japanese army launched a large-scale attack on Jinzhou in the west. On January 2nd of this year, Jinzhou finally fell due to the non-resistance policy of our Northeast authorities. Then they sent a large army to attack Harbin. On February 5th, Harbin was also occupied. Half of the Northeast's territory had been completely seized by the Japanese.

After occupying the Northeast, the Japanese began to implement their second step of the plan, repeating their old drama of destroying Korea. Last December, under the command of the Japanese army, the so-called new provincial government was established in Shenyang. Later, puppet regimes similar to those in Liaoning were established in Jilin and Qiqihar. The so-called local independence movement was successfully carried out. The cry for the establishment of a new state arose in response. During the Tianjin Incident last November, the Japanese took the opportunity to kidnap Puyi, planning to make him the head of the puppet regime. On January 15th of this year, the so-called state-building conference officially opened. At this conference, the date for the establishment of the puppet regime was determined. On February 18th, the newly established Northeast Administrative Committee issued a declaration, announcing the independence of Manchuria and Inner Mongolia. On March 1st, the so-called puppet state of Manchuria was officially proclaimed. In September, the puppet Puyi assumed the puppet position in Changchun. On the 11th, the so-called puppet constitution was promulgated. Thus, this ugly puppet show was completed. On the 15th of this month, Japan further blatantly disregarded everything and officially recognized the puppet state. Since the puppet organization was created single-handedly by the Japanese, it was naturally inevitable for them to create it and recognize it themselves.

However, the atrocities inflicted on us by the Japanese were not limited to the occupation of the Northeast and the crude creation of the puppet state. Last winter, the Japanese repeatedly caused trouble in Fuzhou, Qingdao, and other coastal areas, deliberately provoking incidents. On November 10th, they created the Tianjin Incident. Then, they forced Wang Shuchang, the chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, to sign humiliating conditions. The painful impression given to us by the Shanghai catastrophe of January 28th this year was particularly deep. The war in Shanghai lasted for one month and four days. Under the bombing of Japanese military aircraft and artillery, only ruins and rubble remain in Zhabei, Wusong, Jiangwan, and other places. As for the massacre of our people, it is innumerable. Can we forget this bloody account, these various wounds of repeated whippings? Can we bear to forget them?

If we cannot forget, what should we do? Only strive for self-improvement and strength, seeking self-help and self-salvation through our own efforts.

Our country's biggest mistake in the past year was not being willing to resist violence and defend ourselves with our own strength, but merely appealing to the League of Nations. This policy still seems unwilling to be abandoned until recently. This time, Japan recognized the puppet state, and still only cited the Nine-Power Treaty, issuing a powerless protest as usual. In fact, the lack of capacity of the League of Nations and the Nine-Power Treaty is very obvious, and they definitely cannot respond to our urgent needs. Today, from the perspective of the international situation, the conflict with Japan is becoming increasingly acute with the United States. Japan's occupation of the Northeast directly conflicts with the principle of equal opportunity and open doors held by the United States, giving the United States great stimulation. Therefore, U.S. Secretary of State Stimson made clear accusations against Japan in two speeches. However, the reason why the conflict between the United States and Japan has not erupted immediately is partly because of the issue of war debts between Britain and France, which is unsatisfactory to the United States, and Japan threatened to withdraw from the League of Nations. Britain and France do not want Japan to withdraw from the League of Nations, so the United States is in an isolated position diplomatically and does not dare to take any action rashly. Furthermore, Japan's occupation of our Northeast to attack the Soviet Union is also one of its main functions, and this function is tacitly acknowledged by the great powers. Because of these two reasons, although the contradictions between the United States and Japan are increasing, the final conflict is still early. Under this kind of international situation, appealing to the League of Nations has been disappointing, and appealing to the Nine-Power Treaty will not succeed. Moreover, the problems facing our country in the future are not only a simple Northeast problem, but the difficulty of coping with the situation in the Second World War in two senses. How will our country deal with itself? As the international situation is on the verge of its final transformation, all the tragic phenomena will unfold in order. If our country does not urgently prepare and strive for self-improvement, how can not only the Northeast problem be permanently unresolved, but also how can we survive in the future world war?

A year passes easily. Everything in our country today is no different from a year ago. If this continues, then on this day next year, we may not even be able to make passive commemorations as we do today. A great disaster is coming. If we do not resign ourselves to destruction, then lying on firewood and tasting gall, striving for self-improvement, please begin today.

Conflict Between Liu Zhennian's Troops and Militias in Changping Area

Cao Fulin's Troops Move East and Set Up Headquarters in Weixian

Shen Honglie Sends Marines to Jimo to Prevent Defeated Soldiers

Liu Zhennian Asks Ma Hongkui and Yu Xuezhong to Mediate

Han and Liu's Offices in Beijing Remain Silent on the War Situation

(Qingdao) Liu Zhennian recently levied an additional 400,000 yuan in his defense area, which the people cannot afford. Conflicts between Liu's troops and the militias. Zhao Mingyuan, the commander-in-chief of the Shandong militias, telegraphed the province for help. Han sent Cao Fulin's troops east, and the headquarters were set up in Weixian. The center of the war is in the Changping area. Liu has deployed three defense lines. In recent days, military trains on the Jiaoji Railway have been crowded. Shen Honglie sent marines to Jimo to prevent defeated soldiers from entering the city. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Qingdao) The division and brigade commanders of Han Fuju's troops stationed in Jiaodong had some misunderstandings due to troop rotations with Liu Zhennian's troops. Newspapers took the opportunity to spread rumors, saying that the two sides had contact last night. This city is close to the Jiaoji Railway. Shen Honglie, in order to maintain order, sent a battalion of marines to Chengyang yesterday to defend it. On the afternoon of the 17th, he sent Chief of Staff Xie to Wei to contact Han's generals and find out the truth in order to take precautions. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Beiping) It is said that Han Fuju's Fulin troops stationed in Weixian had a misunderstanding with Liu Zhennian's troops in Pingdu. The reason, it is said, is that the central government issues 500,000 yuan in military expenses to Shandong Province every month. Liu repeatedly asked Han for a monthly payment of 200,000 yuan. Han agreed to issue 120,000 yuan per month. Liu then sent a representative to visit Han, proposing a compromise plan, issuing 145,000 yuan per month. The provincial government failed to issue the full amount. Several days ago, there were various rumors in Jiaodong. Representatives from all parties have been very busy recently. Liu sent representative Zhang Hexuan to Beiping to visit Ma Hongkui and Zhao Fuchen, and went to Tianjin to visit Yu Xuezhong, asking them to mediate. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Nanjing) According to foreign telegrams here, there is talk of a conflict between Han Fuju's and Liu Zhennian's troops, which has attracted much attention from all walks of life. According to Han's office in Beijing, this rumor is feared to be propaganda deliberately made by the Japanese. According to Liu's office in Beijing, the office has not received any telegrams regarding this news and it is difficult to verify. A telegram has been sent to inquire, and the truth will be known by the morning of the 18th. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Jinan) Han's representative, Liu Xizhong, will go to Ping today to visit Zhang. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Qingdao) According to a telegram received from a certain place, the militia army under Han Fuju, stationed along the Jiaoji Railway in Gaomi, Weixian, Pingdu, and Changle, and the Liu Zhennian army in that area suddenly started fighting last night. The reason is due to mutual antagonism over the issue of security zones. It is said that the militia was secretly ordered by Han Fuju to resolve the Liu Zhennian army, which has been taking a neutral attitude. In Pingdu, there are 20 Japanese residents. Japanese officials have negotiated with Han Fuju's army and the local public security bureau regarding the protection of their lives and property. (Telegram from the 17th, Electric News Agency)

(Nanjing) The Chinese here have not heard of the rumor spread by the Japanese that Shandong Chairman Han Fuju and Yantai Liu Zhennian's troops have clashed. Reuters' Nanjing correspondent inquired with Han and Liu's representatives in Beijing tonight. They all found this statement very strange. They all have private wireless stations and communicate frequently with Shandong Province, but they have not received any such report. Both representatives have now telegraphed Jinan and Yantai separately to find out the truth. (Reuters dispatch from the 17th)

Feng and Wang Lead Troops to Besiege Jilin City

Japanese Troops in Jilin City Isolated, Jidun and Jihai Traffic Interrupted

Peng Zhenduo's Troops Occupy Honglu and Liujiazi, Attacking Jinzhou

(Beiping) A person from Jilin talked about how Feng Zhanhai and Wang Delin personally led their troops to attack Jilin City. Feng's troops have arrived in the Huanshiling area behind Beishan on the west side of Jilin City and near the Motianling area in the northwest. Wang's troops have attacked the Tuanshazi area on the east side, taking a three-sided encirclement. The Japanese army has dug trenches on the east and west sides of the provincial capital. The Japanese troops in the city are isolated and without support. The Jidun and Jihai roads are both impassable. The two sides are in fierce battle. The righteous army is very powerful. Feng and Wang's troops have occupied various places, only four li away from the city. Although the Japanese army has set up an airfield north of the city, it has failed due to the tight defenses of the righteous army. Jilin City can be recovered soon. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Beiping) The troops under Wang Delin and the volunteer army under Feng Zhanhai jointly attacked Jilin. Therefore, the railway traffic between Jilin, Hailun, and Jilin, Dunhua has been interrupted. The Jilin Manchu army is very embarrassed. Ma Zhanshan telegraphed to request troops to be sent outside the pass to suppress the rebels. Ma's representative brought his personal letter and visited various dignitaries here, asking for assistance with funds and military supplies. (Reuters dispatch from the 17th)

(Shanhaiguan) The Wang and Feng troops attacking Jilin City, with the internal support of a battalion of the Jilin Provincial Guard, once attacked the Yongji city wall on the night of the 14th, and fought a fierce battle with the Japanese rebel army. They withdrew on the afternoon of the 15th. Countless rebels were annihilated in this battle, and many spoils of war were seized. Currently, our army is still gathered in the suburbs, surrounding the provincial capital. The Japanese rebel army is holding on to the provincial capital, urgently awaiting reinforcements. Battles are now taking place everywhere in Jilin Province. Ning'an County on the east road has been occupied by the righteous army, and is engaged in fierce fighting with the Itoda brigade of the Japanese army. The Shenhai Road is still interrupted. The Eastern Border Army is advancing from Xi'an to Yitong County on the Jilin border, coordinating with the Jilin army to meet in the pseudo-capital. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Beiping) Peng Zhenduo, the commander-in-chief of the First Military Region of the National Salvation Army, and Dong Rongji, commander of the First Route, Bai Yunfei, deputy commander, and Wang Yongliang, brigade commander of the Second Brigade, have occupied Liujiazi in Honglu County near Jinzhou. They are now attacking Jinzhou, and have suffered losses due to heavy artillery fire from the Japanese army. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Guerrillas Enter Shenyang City

(Beiping) Foreign news reports that a large number of guerrillas have sneaked into Shenyang City, waiting for an opportunity to respond to the righteous army and attack the Japanese rebel armies. The security is extremely tight. Armored vehicles are dispatched to patrol the streets, and the shop windows are mostly not removed. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Dong Rongji's Troops Attack Gaotaizi

(Beiping) Dong Rongji of the 11th Route Righteous Army led more than a hundred soldiers to attack Gaotaizi on the morning of the 10th. There were only a dozen Japanese soldiers there. Eight enemies were killed and two captured, and five rifles were captured. Only one of our soldiers was injured. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Japanese Army Uses Dum-Dum Bullets

(Beiping) The Japanese army used Dum-Dum bullets in battles with the Righteous Army in the Nuer River and other places in Jinzhou. Several officers of the Righteous Army were seriously ulcerated due to Dum-Dum bullet wounds and have come to Beiping and Tianjin for treatment. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Geng Jizhou's Troops Attack Shenyang

(Beiping) Geng Jizhou's troops of the 4th Route of the Righteous Army in western Liaoning, about 6,000 people, attacked the west side of the Dasibei Gate in Shenyang this morning. The fighting was quite fierce. Tang Juwu's troops and other routes of the Righteous Army in eastern Liaoning also launched attacks and came into contact with the Japanese army in Fushun, Dabeiying, and Xiling. Fierce battles are expected to break out within days. Wang Naijiang's troops of the 17th Detachment of Geng Jizhou's Righteous Army are active in the Qinghemen area north of Yixian. Xiu Jizeng's troops of the 13th Detachment are currently engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese army in Chaoyang Temple. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Jinzhou Transferred to the Rehe Border

(Beiping) After Japan recognized the puppet state, the Mabe unit of the 8th Division of the Japanese Army stationed in Jinzhou was transferred to Chaoyang Temple and Yixian. A total of 300 Japanese troops are stationed at Chaoyang Temple. An airfield is being built near the station. Sandbags and military telephones are set up on the station platform, directly connected to Jinzhou. Japanese armored vehicles are parked in the station, and all soldiers stay in the vehicles every night. The army from Chaoyang Temple to Nanling Station, Nanling and Koubeiyingzi, are guarded by the Rehe Road Protection Team. The train from Jinzhou to Beipiao only goes to Chaoyang Temple. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Sun Guoru's Troops Advance on Suizhong

(Beiping) A guest from Suizhong said that Sun Guoru's 500-strong Righteous Army set out towards Suizhong on the 14th. Villages such as Chenjiatun were destroyed by enemy bombing one after another. Over 400 militiamen voluntarily joined the war and were willing to serve as vanguards. At 8 pm, they besieged the city, but all the city gates were blocked by the Japanese army. Only the southeast gates had two heavy machine guns each. The eastern gate station was surrounded by electrified wire mesh and machine gun fortifications. The attacks for two hours made no progress. Close to the west, hand-held grenades were used to explode on the city wall. The Japanese army could not hold out and retreated, suffering many casualties. After dawn, when the Righteous Army troops retreated to Luzhaogou, more than 400 Japanese soldiers with 16 machine guns, 12 artillery pieces, and 20 cars attacked the villages north of the units. Enemy machine guns and artillery bombarded civilian houses indiscriminately. The militia fought desperately, and the enemy army was defeated, killing more than 20 enemies and capturing 25 rifles and 1 submachine gun. Later, two aircraft arrived, dropping five bombs, and each team stopped the pursuit. More than 120 houses in the village were destroyed by bombing, with heavy losses. The enemy's mountain artillery destroyed one artillery piece. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Capital Garrison Department Recommends

That National Calamity Conferences in Various Schools Be Cancelled

(Nanjing) The Capital Garrison Department, because the anti-Japanese associations of various schools in the capital scheduled a National Calamity Memorial Meeting for the September 18th Incident at Zhongda on the 18th, fearing that reactionary elements would take the opportunity to make trouble during this period of martial law, sent a special commissioner to negotiate with the association to recommend cancellation. The association has sent letters to various schools to suspend the meeting and stop all publicity and fundraising activities. (Special dispatch from the 18th)

Swatow National Salvation Society Inspects Goods

Japanese Consul Protests to the Municipal Government in Swatow

(Swatow) Chen Tingyang and Song, who were carrying goods of animosity privately, were captured and paraded through the streets by inspectors of the National Salvation Society. The Japanese consul personally went to the municipal government to submit a protest letter, stating that the 4th branch of the Public Security Bureau took custody of innocent people, infringing upon the freedom of foreign businessmen's business. The municipal government sent a letter to the party headquarters, asking them to avoid relationships with foreigners in the future. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Japanese Troops Conduct Military Exercises in Tianjin and Yuguan

Yuguan Authorities Question the Japanese Side

Plainclothes Team in the Japanese Concession in Tianjin Increases to 2,000

(Tianjin) The plainclothes team in the Japanese concession has now increased to more than 2,000 people. It was originally planned to launch an incident on September 18th, but the plot was detected by our police and constitution, so it was decided to abandon it. The Japanese army, from 9 pm on the 16th to 4 am on the 17th, conducted street fighting exercises in the Japanese concession, and extinguished the street lights, causing extreme tension among the people. Mayor Zhou Longguang persuaded the Japanese consul not to conduct exercises in the suburbs on the 18th to avoid misunderstandings. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

(Beiping) The Japanese army in Yuguan is heavily guarded, with sentries released day and night. Armed Japanese police patrol the station. (Telegram from the 17th)

(Shanhaiguan) More than 200 Japanese troops stationed in Yuguan mobilized this morning at 9:00 am, divided into two teams, offensive and defensive, and conducted blank-firing exercises. One team went from the south gate of Yucheng to the station, and the other went from the west gate to the Shi River. The exercises lasted for two hours before the matter was settled. Our side was not notified in advance, causing merchants to be alarmed and suspicious. A few merchants closed their doors. Our military police maintained order, and the local area is now as peaceful as usual. This type of exercise is the first since the Shenyang Incident. The local authorities are deeply concerned that misunderstandings may easily arise, have questioned the Japanese side, and requested that it not be held again. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

This order. League of Nations

Secretariat to Be Reorganized

Forming a Situation Dominated by Britain and France

Poland Seeks to Re-elect as Semi-Permanent Councillor

National News Agency, Geneva, 17th – According to those who are well informed, the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Briton Drummond, will step down after this session of the League of Nations General Assembly. Britain and France have already agreed to appoint the current Deputy Secretary-General, Frenchman Avenol, to succeed him. At that time, the Secretariat will also be reorganized, and the three deputy secretaries from Italy, Germany, and Japan will be removed, leaving only the Secretary-General, the Deputy Secretary-General, and the Accountant. It is said that the Deputy Secretary-General will become a purely nominal position, intended for an Italian, and the Accountant will be a Briton, but his powers will be expanded to counterbalance the power of France and Germany after they have acquired the Secretary-General position. It is expected that this reorganization plan will be submitted to the League of Nations Council at this session. Germany and Italy are expected to protest this attempt to strip the two countries of their power and create a situation in the League of Nations where Britain and France have equal shares. However, the German government has anticipated that this change will be implemented and has already indicated that it intends to appoint League of Nations Deputy Secretary Dufour-Feronce as the minister to Portugal.

German Written Statement

Not Participating in Disarmament Work

Firmly Refusing to Relinquish Demand for Equality

Determined to Conduct Oral Negotiations with France

Believing that Exchange of Official Documents is of No Practical Help

Havas, Berlin, 16th – The letter from German Foreign Minister Neurath to Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, on the 14th of this month, has recently been officially released. The letter stated, "Any solutions to the disarmament issue must be applicable to Germany before Germany can be asked to participate in the Disarmament Conference to discuss the various disarmament clauses that should be included in the final convention. As long as the above conditions are not met, Germany cannot be asked to participate in negotiations. The Federal Government is eager to realize the conditions for Germany to cooperate with the Disarmament Conference, so it is conducting negotiations through diplomatic procedures to find a way to achieve equality of armaments. Unexpectedly, Germany's various efforts have not yielded any satisfactory results to date, which the Federal Government deeply regrets. Under these circumstances, the Minister has to inform you that the government cannot attend the meeting of the Disarmament Bureau on the 21st of this month as scheduled. We hope for your understanding. However, our country will continue to pay attention to the work of the Disarmament Conference, and its future attitude will also depend on the situation of the conference."

Reuters, Berlin, 16th – Reuters learned today that the German government does not want to reply to the French government's letter refusing Germany's demand for equality of armaments. Although the German government believes that continuing to exchange official documents will not help solve the problem, it stated that it is willing to conduct oral diplomatic negotiations. It has now informed all relevant countries of this intention.

Havas, London, 16th – British Prime Minister MacDonald departed for Chequers Villa this afternoon, but how the British Cabinet will decide on Germany's demand for equality of armaments has not yet been announced. Danube River

Economic Recovery Conference

Compromise on Grain Export Issue

Reuters, Stresa, 16th – The greatest result of the Stresa Conference, which considered the economic recovery of Eastern and Central Europe, is probably the subsidy for Danube River grain exports, with a subsidy of one Swiss franc per 112 pounds. The cost is borne by European taxpayers. It is heard that the Agricultural Economic Committee organized by the conference has agreed on the following two points: (1) The export quota for each country that has surplus grain available for export and is eligible for subsidies will be determined by the average export quota of the past three years, with a total amount of approximately 10,080,000,000 pounds; (2) European countries must donate to the subsidy fund, not limited to importing countries.

French Debt Conversion Plan

Passed by the Chamber of Deputies, to be Implemented Soon

Reuters, Paris, 17th – The French debt conversion bill was passed by the Chamber of Deputies this morning with 540 votes to 48. The Chamber of Deputies met all night to make the bill law on Sunday.

Reuters, Paris, 16th – France's plan to swap new bonds for old bonds is about to be implemented. The new bonds will start with a 4.5% interest rate to replace several types of old bonds with 5%, 6%, and 7% interest rates, with a total amount of 85,000,000,000 francs. A special meeting of the National Assembly has been convened today to propose a bill for this plan. The 4.5% interest rate new bonds will be effective from November 1st of this year and will begin to be repaid by lottery or purchase starting in 1939, and will be paid off within 75 years after issuance, and will be exempt from all special taxes. Holders of these old bonds who do not apply for redemption within six days will be deemed to have acknowledged the exchange of new bonds.

Havas, La Paz, 17th – The Bolivian government declared to the neutral commission that the country is prepared to cease hostilities.

Death of Renowned British Medical Scientist

Sir Ross, Inventor of New Malaria Treatment

Havas, London, 16th – Sir Ross, the scholar renowned globally for his discoveries in the field of malaria, has recently passed away at the age of 71. Ross began his research on malaria in 1892, and later continued his exploration around the world. He was the first to prove that malaria is caused by mosquito bites and invented a treatment for malaria that is popular worldwide today. He was elected as a member of numerous scientific organizations during his lifetime, and was awarded medals by various countries around the world.

British Aviator

Sets New Altitude Record

Reaching 45,000 Feet

Reuters, London, 17th – Captain Uwins, a famous aviator who served as a pilot in the Royal Air Force during the European War, flew a 550-horsepower aircraft over the Severn River basin today, ascending to approximately 45,000 feet (approximately eight miles and ninety-two yards), exceeding the previous aviation altitude record by over 1,500 feet. Uwins took off from Bristol Aerodrome and continued to fly for over two hours. Because the weather in the sky was very cold, he was equipped with special oxygen extraction equipment, and his goggles, gloves, and clothing were heated electrically. He then landed in Evesham, Worcestershire. His record now needs to be verified by the Royal Aero Club.

News in Brief

Commemoration of the September 18th National Crisis 12

A Heartfelt Appeal to the Nation by Ma Zhanshan

The heartbreaking September 18th Incident, without realizing it, has passed for a whole year. In this year, my compatriots in the Northeast have suffered the pain of national subjugation, which has only intensified. My loyal and patriotic soldiers have sacrificed themselves in the Black Mountains and White Waters, striving for national glory, fighting for national dignity, and upholding justice and righteousness for humanity. They have fallen one after another, following closely without interruption. My elders, brothers, sisters, and female cousins at home and abroad have been concerned about the fall of the Northeast territory, have helped the displaced compatriots of the Northeast, and have given material and spiritual encouragement to the front-line soldiers who have risked their lives to kill the enemy. Their benevolence and righteousness have been boundless. Zhanshan, awaiting punishment in the military, has received much favor. However, looking back on the results of the struggle and sacrifice of the past year, not only have we failed to expel the strong enemy and restore our rivers and mountains, but the puppet state has also calmly taken the stage. There is no matter more heartbreaking than this. Today, on the day of the commemoration of the September 18th National Crisis, Zhanshan dares to sincerely appeal to my patriotic compatriots: As long as the lost territory of the Northeast is not recovered for a single day, Zhanshan will not cease fighting for a single day. Even if I have only my last bullet, I will kill one enemy to repay the country. This heart and this will have already been stated in telegrams. Now, I will again respectfully report to the nation the progress of Zhanshan's resistance against Japan over the past ten months, as well as my determination to fight in the future.

Last year's September 18th Incident was by no means accidental. Japan had been planning and plotting to invade and occupy Manchuria and Mongolia long before the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95. However, due to the obstruction of the powers, they did not have the opportunity. Therefore, they endured for decades until today. Now, all countries in the world are facing a severe economic crisis, and they are all busy dealing with the financial and economic problems of their own countries and related countries, and have no time to care about the Far East. The Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan has not yet been completed, and it cannot abandon its national construction plan to compete with Japan for foreign markets. Moreover, its national strength is insufficient, and even if it wants to compete with Japan for dominance, it cannot be sure of victory. In addition, our country is plagued by natural disasters and banditry, which are widespread throughout the country, and the national defense of the Northeast is also inadequate. All kinds of reasons are enough to arouse the Japanese people's covetous thoughts. Therefore, they brazenly disregarded everything and carried out the violent occupation of Shenyang on September 18th. First, they disarmed our troops and seized our political power, and then they directed the traitors to organize local maintenance associations and establish autonomous guidance departments, causing Jilin and Heilongjiang to fall. Then, they further encouraged the puppets to establish the so-called Manchuria, in order to achieve their final goal of invading Manchuria and Mongolia. The League of Nations Covenant is not to be feared, the Nine-Power Treaty is not to be counted, and the warnings of the powers and the resistance of the Chinese people are not to be worried about. It is like having gold in front of them, only seeing the gold and not seeing the people. Their greed is hateful and their viciousness is fearful. As for why the Japanese dared to take the risk of injustice to forcibly occupy our three northeastern provinces, there is a reason. Tanaka Giichi's memorial on the positive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia has already explained it in detail. It said, “If we want to conquer China, we must first conquer Manchuria and Mongolia. If we want to conquer the world, we must first conquer China. If China is completely conquered by our country, other foreign nations such as Central and Small Asia, India, and the South Seas will fear and respect us and surrender to us, so that the world will know that East Asia is our East Asia, and will never dare to invade us. This is the legacy of Emperor Meiji, and it is also a necessary thing for the existence of our Japanese Empire.” This is from a political point of view. Japan's ambition is to use the occupation of Manchuria and Mongolia as the first step in conquering the world. As for the economic significance, it said, “If our rights in Manchuria and Mongolia can truly be in our hands, then we can use Manchuria and Mongolia as a base, use the mask of trade to sweep across China's four hundred and odd states, and then use the rights in Manchuria and Mongolia as a command tower to seize China's resources, and use China's resources to conquer India and the South Seas Islands, as well as Central and Small Asia and Europe. The first key to our Yamato nation's desire to set foot on the Asian continent is to grasp the rights and interests of Manchuria and Mongolia. Moreover, the final victor relies on food, the prosperity of industry relies on raw materials, and the fulfillment of national power relies on a vast Chinese territory. If our rights in Manchuria and Mongolia are expanded with a positive policy, we can solve all kinds of major national factors, not to mention that our country's annual surplus of 700,000 people can also be solved at the same time. If we want to implement the Showa Restoration and achieve the permanent prosperity of our empire, we must only focus on the principle of actively pursuing the rights and interests of Manchuria and Mongolia.” This is the truth about the Japanese invasion of Manchuria and Mongolia, which was completely revealed by Tanaka's mouth. Yet they still deceive the world by saying that they have no ambition for territory. Who would believe it? Because of this, if we want to subdue these stubborn bandits and protect our sovereignty, we must fight them with force, and it is not enough to frustrate the enemy's edge and kill the enemy's spirit. This is why Zhanshan had the battle of Jiangqiao to kill the bandits on November 4th of last year. Since then, there has hardly been a day when I have not been in the midst of guns and bullets, advancing and retreating, fighting and resting. It has been more than ten months since I telegraphed my resistance. Fortunately, with the assistance of the people and the dedication of the soldiers, Zhanshan has been able to support the critical situation with an isolated army in the border region. Even the ruthless artillery fire of the stubborn bandits cannot do anything to my brothers with red hearts and righteous courage.

Earlier, after the Japanese bandits occupied Changchun, they used Zhang Hai Peng to advance into Heihe. At that time, Zhanshan was ordered to act as chairman. On October 3rd, the Japanese consul stationed in Jiang province came to visit, saying that the Japanese army would repair the Nenjiang Iron Bridge, which I firmly refused. On the morning of the 4th, a large Japanese army attacked me and was defeated and fled. On the morning of the 5th, the enemy army attacked again, with more intense artillery fire. Our army fought bravely at night, killing three or four hundred bandits, and the morale of the army was greatly boosted. After suffering a setback, the enemy increased its artillery force by more than a thousand men and transferred them from the Siping-Taonan Railway to Jiangqiao Station. Japanese troops from various places gathered and crossed the river at night, and countless of them were sunk by us. On the 6th, the enemy further increased its strength and used armored vehicles to cover its advance. The firepower of airplanes and artillery was the most intense. Our army felt great difficulty and had to retreat to Daxing Station. Then, we joined forces to counterattack and surrounded the enemy, and after a fierce battle all day, we were able to repel the enemy. On the 7th, more enemies arrived, and we also increased our reinforcements and cooperated to attack, killing thousands of enemies, and the bodies were all over the field. The bandit crowd was defeated and fled across the river in a panic. We then restored the first line of defense, so the front line was more solid, and the enemy did not dare to underestimate our army. After the Japanese were defeated, they hurriedly transferred the Hasegawa Brigade and the Amano Brigade from Changchun to fight. In addition, cavalry artillery came to support in turn, and dozens of aircraft bombed in rotation. Our army fought bravely to be the first, and after half an hour of hand-to-hand combat, they finally repelled the stubborn bandits. As a result of the fierce battles on the 6th and 7th, the enemy army suffered a disastrous defeat, and our losses were also not light. It is estimated that the number of enemy troops killed and wounded in this battle was about two thousand. After the enemy army was defeated on the 7th, they retreated to the south of the Nenjiang Bridge to wait for reinforcements before attacking again, so there was nothing peaceful before the 11th. On the 12th, the great battle began again. Zhanshan had sent two telegrams, Yu and Yu, to inform the people of the country of this battle. On the 12th, the enemy army attacked me with a force of seven thousand infantrymen. At the same time, Honjo sent a letter to Zhanshan, demanding (1) Zhanshan to step down, (2) the Heihe army to withdraw from Qiqihar, and (3) a part of the Japanese army to advance to Angangxi, and set a deadline for a reply before 12 o'clock that night. At that time, Zhanshan had received orders from Vice Commander Zhang to resolutely reject them and prepare to resist to the death. On the night of the 12th, the Japanese infantry and artillery attacked our defense line. On the morning of the 13th, they attacked our cavalry position with a small force. On the morning of the 14th, the artillerymen detoured from the west and launched a fierce attack on our cavalry defense line. The Japanese army opened fire on the front to contain our infantry and artillery forces. Our defense line shook. Fortunately, the reinforcements of the Tu Quan Sheng Regiment arrived, and the entire regiment charged into hand-to-hand combat. The sound of killing shook the sky, and the bandit army was greatly frightened and fled in a panic, with countless dead and wounded. Since this defeat, the Japanese knew that our army was good at fighting, so they greatly increased their reinforcements, and airplanes, artillery, tanks, field guns, and various weapons were used together. They also transferred the troops stationed in Korea and joined the front line. From the 15th to the 18th, after four days of great battles, we were unable to support it due to our lack of troops and weak equipment. Therefore, on the 18th, we had to lead our troops to withdraw from Heihe and stationed in Keshan. During the retreat, the Japanese army pursued along the way with 20,000 troops and were ambushed twice, killing countless enemies. Then, because Keshan was too small, they led the majority of the troops to Hailun, where the provincial government headquarters were located, and Keshan and Baiquan were used as the second line of defense. The process of retreating has been reported to the whole country in a clever telegram in November. After Zhanshan arrived in Hailun, he actively replenished his military supplies to make a final resistance. Soon after the battle of Harbin broke out, the Japanese enemy again attacked Lindian, Yi'an, Keshan and other counties with heavy troops, so they sent troops to block and attack on the one hand, and assisted Ding and Li on the other hand. Unexpectedly, the Heihe army had not yet arrived in Harbin, and the troops of Ding and Li had retreated one after another. After the Japanese bandits occupied my Harbin, they learned that my army was divided to assist Ding and Li, so they drove elite troops to take Hailun, in order to eliminate my army's strength. At that time, my army had a strong enemy pressing in front of them, and no important passes to defend behind them. Ammunition was scarce and reinforcements were cut off, and the situation was extremely critical. Since Zhanshan resisted Japan, he had long put life and death out of his mind. However, the strong bandits had not been eliminated, and the national crisis was urgent. The enemy was strong and we were weak, and the bandits were numerous and we were few. If we were to sacrifice the country's strength and steal personal loyalty and national honor, we would be a traitor to the country. Therefore, I resolutely held a secret meeting with Ding, Li and others in the county town of Hulan to discuss countermeasures. They all believed that the crisis of survival was imminent, and there was no time to waste. If we wanted to solve the current difficulties, we could only use a trick to deceive the enemy and slow down their pursuit, and we could save our strength and wait for the troops in Guannei to come out, and then raise the banner of righteousness to act as an internal response to achieve the effect of a pincer attack. And the various conspiracies of the Japanese bandits to invade us could also be detected at any time. After the meeting was decided, they proposed the following surrender conditions to the enemy general Domon's division: 1. Stop all military actions against Jilin and Heilongjiang. 2. Do not kill the people. 3. Replenish ammunition and military pay. The draft of these conditions was carried to Harbin by the traitorous Chinese traitors Zhao Zhongren and Han Yunkai. Domon fully accepted it and asked the two Chinese traitors, Zhao and Han, to return to Hulan to report and urge Zhanshan to personally go to Harbin to meet with Domon. Domon held a banquet at the Hotel Matier, without any suspicion, and urged him to return to the province as soon as possible to preside over the military and civilian affairs. Zhanshan returned to Hulan that night and appointed Zhao and Han as representatives to stay in Harbin to handle affairs. Immediately, he invited Ding and Li to report the results of the contact with Domon and secretly decided to expand his strength and wait for an opportunity to act. They were actively trained and ordered the guard regiment to move to Hulan to protect the Huhai Railway, and the name of the guard regiment was abolished to cover up the eyes and ears of the Japanese bandits. The ammunition and clothing stored in Hailun were moved to Longmen (about 400 miles north of Hailun). All the important documents of the military office were handed over to the commander-in-chief of the People's Army for safekeeping. The talented staff and adjutants of the military office who advocated resistance against Japan were all dismissed, but secretly they were assigned the responsibility of military training in the People's Army, or served as leaders. Plan to Raise 500,000 Yuan to Purchase Six Aircraft

Jinan Correspondence: In modern warfare, the air force is the only sharp weapon. All countries in the East and West are actively expanding it and progressing rapidly. However, our country's air force is very weak. Since the outbreak of the Northeast Incident, the national crisis has become increasingly urgent. In order to consolidate national defense and resist foreign aggression, aviation salvation associations have been initiated in various places, with people freely donating funds to purchase aircraft and form salvation aviation troops. Shandong Province connects the north and south, is adjacent to a strong enemy in the east, has many important ports and numerous ports. It is an important area in military terms and is of great importance to national defense. Recently, more than 20 people, including Wang Zhanyuan, Jin Yun'e, Ma Liang, Xin Zhujiu, chairman of the provincial business association, Miao Xingcai, chairman of the Jinan Flour Industry Association, He Dingyuan, president of the Bank of China, Lu Tingzhuan, president of the Bank of Communications, Zhao Xinru, manager of the Shandong Official Pawnshop, and Zhang Shuheng, chairman of the Jinan Chamber of Commerce, initiated and organized the Shandong Salvation Aviation Association. They plan to raise donations to purchase aircraft and hand them over to the provincial government to form the Shandong Salvation Aviation Army, so that they can assist the navy and army in resisting foreign aggression when the country is in trouble. The association has been brewing for many days and is now organized. On the evening of the 13th, the initiators held a banquet for the province's party and government leaders at the Bank of Communications, explaining the purpose of the association and asking for assistance in carrying it out. Zhang Weicun, the province's rectification committee, and others greatly praised it. Immediately, Jin Yun'e, Wang Zhanyuan, Zhao Xinru, Miao Xingcun, Shi Shaoxian, Ma Liang, Xin Zhujiu, Zhang Shuheng, He Dingyuan, Lu Tingzhuan, Guo Zuoting and other 21 people were designated as preparation committee members, responsible for planning and carrying out the project. It was decided to hold the first preparation committee meeting at Daguanyuan at 3 pm on the 16th to discuss the issuance of donation announcements and widely solicit donations so that aircraft can be purchased and the air force can be organized as soon as possible. According to the initiators of the association, it is difficult to predict the results of future fundraising, but in any case, the funds raised must be more than 500,000 yuan, which can buy six aircraft, so that a team of salvation aviation troops can be organized. If more donations are received, all of them will be used to purchase aircraft and will not be used for other purposes (15th).

Chiang Kai-shek's Letter to Six Provincial Governments to Prepare Grain Storage 14

Also Encourage Rural Animal Husbandry

Hankou Correspondence: In order to prepare grain storage and encourage animal husbandry, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent a letter to the chairmen of six provinces, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei, on the 15th to instruct them on the methods. The original letter is as follows: "Brothers Mo San, Yong An, Li Qing, Tian Yi, Yun Qiao, and Ling Bing, I have learned that the system of grain storage has been passed down from ancient times to the present, without any change. Even in the late Qing Dynasty, after the great chaos of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, all provinces in the southeast, whether in poor rural areas or remote areas, had public and private granaries with sufficient grain storage. In lean years, they were released on credit, and in years of famine, they were sold at a fixed price, so even in years of drought and flood, the people did not suffer from hunger. Since the past ten years, wars and bandit disasters have continued incessantly, and the private storage systems of various provinces have been largely destroyed. If there is a slight famine, the fields are filled with cries of sorrow. Every time I think about this, I feel pain. It is imperative to repair and restore it as soon as possible. In the past, Confucius said that in politics, sufficient food comes before sufficient soldiers. Guan Zhong said that in governance, the four pillars must be based on the reality of the granaries. In recent times, European and American countries have sufficient preparations and detailed statistics for the national food supply. It is known that the people's food is the source of governance and chaos in a country and is related to the strength or weakness of national power. Therefore, I especially send this letter to my brother, urging him to supervise the counties under his jurisdiction, take advantage of the harvest season to actively prepare grain storage, and take the total population of each county as a ratio, and set aside at least three months' worth of food for storage. The quantity must not be vague, and the deadline must not be delayed. All the old, daily-average warehouses in the counties, townships, and cities that still maintain a good system and have no loopholes should continue to follow the old rules and be carefully maintained. Those that have been destroyed or even completely destroyed should also be strictly reorganized and ordered to be restored. All of these facilities should be completed within three months. Supervise and urge the departments to complete the work and strictly order the counties to report to the provincial government on schedule with accurate statistics as the standard for the provincial grain storage. In addition, rural animal husbandry, such as cattle, sheep, mules, horses, as well as raising chickens and pigs, are also supplementary foods and have a significant relationship with rural cultivation, transportation, and economy. It is also hoped that new scientific methods will be adopted to improve breeding and formulate reward rules to promote animal husbandry in a practical way. For families with a particularly large number of livestock, cattle, and horses, they should be given special awards, so that the people will be inspired and animal husbandry will flourish. Then, the abundance of materials and people will be a profound contribution to increasing the strength of the people. In short, grain storage is enough to prevent changes and stabilize the people, and animal husbandry is enough to enrich the people and provide for their needs. Although the two seem insignificant, they are both the foundation of governance. Please follow the instructions in this letter and implement them seriously. In addition to sending separate letters to the provincial governments of (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei) to supervise and carry out the work at the same time, this letter is specially sent to you for compliance, and I hope that you will report the progress of the work at any time so that I can assess the situation." (September 16th)

Legislative Yuan Passes 15

Regulations on Rewarding Industrial Technology

The Legislative Yuan held its 202nd meeting on the morning of the 17th and passed the Provisional Regulations on Rewarding Industrial Technology, with a total of 29 articles. The full text is recorded as follows: (Article 1) Any citizen of the Republic of China who is the first to invent industrial goods or methods may apply for rewards in accordance with these Regulations. (Article 2) Those who are rewarded in accordance with these Regulations shall enjoy a patent right for ten or five years. The patent right in the preceding paragraph shall cover the entire country. (Article 3) Rewards shall not be granted in any of the following circumstances: (1) There is the same invention for which a reward has been approved earlier. (2) It is harmful to public order, good customs, or hygiene. (Article 4) No patent right shall be granted for any invention that is necessary for military secrecy, but the government shall give a reasonable remuneration. (Article 5) A person who receives a reward for an invention may apply for an additional reward for a new invention of the original goods or method during the term of his patent right, but the term shall expire at the expiration of the original patent right. (Article 6) Any person who uses another person's goods or method and makes a new invention during the term of the patent right may apply for a reward, but the new inventor shall give the original inventor a reasonable compensation or agree to jointly manufacture it. The original inventor may not refuse without a legitimate reason. (Article 7) If, after an invention is rewarded, the original inventor and another person make the same re-invention and apply at the same time, only the original inventor shall be rewarded. (Article 8) If two or more persons make the same invention and apply separately, the person who applies first shall be rewarded. If they apply at the same time, it shall be determined by the agreement of the applicants. If the agreement fails, no reward shall be given. (Article 9) If any person applies for a reward in accordance with these Regulations and a part of his invention is the same as another application, the same part shall be rewarded to the person who applied first. (Article 10) When applying in the name of a company or jointly in the name of two or more persons, the name of the inventor shall be stated and a document proving the right to apply shall be attached. (Article 11) The right to apply for a reward and the patent right may be assigned or inherited. (Article 12) If an invention is made at the entrustment of another person or at the expense of an employer, the patent right shall be jointly owned by both parties. (Article 13) When a patent right is jointly owned, the patent right may not be exercised without the consent of each co-owner, but if there is a contract, it shall be governed by the contract. (Article 14) Applications for rewards shall be made to the Ministry of Industry. After examination and confirmation, a certificate shall be issued and the term of the patent right shall be calculated from the date of issuance of the certificate. (Article 15) If an applicant disagrees with the rejection of his application, he may apply for review within 30 days after the delivery of the decision. (Article 16) When an application is reviewed and found to be rewardable, it shall be announced immediately. Interested parties may raise objections within six months from the date of the announcement. (Article 17) If no one raises an objection after the expiration of the announcement period in the preceding article, the review shall be confirmed. (Article 18) A patent right shall be revoked in any of the following circumstances and the certificate shall be recovered: (1) It violates the provisions of Articles 1 and 3 of these Regulations. (2) The manufacture has not been carried out for two years after receiving the reward and has not been approved by the Ministry of Industry. (3) The business has been suspended for more than two years during the term of the patent right without any reason and has not been approved by the Ministry of Industry. (4) Approval was obtained by fraudulent means. (Article 19) When the term of the patent right expires or is revoked in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article, the Ministry of Industry shall announce it. (Article 20) If a patent right is revoked and its additional reward is revoked, it shall be regarded as an independent patent right and a separate certificate shall be issued, which shall remain in effect until the expiration of the patent right. (Article 21) When the term of the patent right expires, it may be extended with the approval of the Ministry of Industry and an additional certificate shall be issued, but it shall be limited to one time and shall not exceed the term of the original patent right. (Article 22) When a patent right is assigned or inherited, a certificate shall be issued by the Ministry of Industry. (Article 23) Any person who counterfeits an invention and damages the patent right of another person shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than three years and may also be fined not more than 5,000 yuan. (Article 24) Any person who imitates an invention or steals its method and damages the patent right of another person shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than two years and may also be fined not more than 3,000 yuan. (Article 25) Any person who knowingly sells or displays for sale an article that is counterfeited or imitated shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than six months, detention, or a fine of not more than 1,000 yuan. (Article 26) The crimes in the preceding three articles shall be prosecuted only upon complaint by the victim. (Article 27) The certificate fee for the patent right shall not exceed 100 yuan, and the certificate fee for extending the term shall not exceed 200 yuan, which may be paid in installments. No other fees may be charged other than the foregoing. (Article 28) The detailed rules for the implementation of these Regulations shall be determined by the Ministry of Industry. (Article 29) These Regulations shall come into force from the date of promulgation.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 16

Dispute over Standards for Collecting Land Survey Fees: The County Government, acting upon instructions from provincial authorities, has ordered the survey of farmland and the collection of land survey expenses under the land tax, charging one dime per mu. For areas less than one mu, it is calculated as one mu, and the collection will continue for three years, with the funds being saved and used for the purpose. However, businesses in the county claim that the provincial method calculates one fen per mu as two mu, and 0.9 mu is also calculated as two mu, resulting in an uneven distribution of burdens. Farms with fragmented land also have separate calculations for each share and fraction. They should immediately unite all businesses in the county and petition the province to fight for a fair system. It was decided that a meeting would be held at 2 PM today (the 17th) at the First District Office to discuss the matter. Over one hundred people attended, and Zhong Taichi was elected chairman. The discussion points were: (1) Regarding the provincial regulations, a resolution was passed to send representatives to the county to inquire about the matter. Wu Juchi, Xi Qianzeng, Du Jinhou, Zhu Shujian, and Zhong Taichi were appointed as the five representatives to go to the County Government to transcribe the provincial regulations. (2) Regarding the standard for collecting land survey fees, a resolution was passed to collect the fees according to the land value tax method, verifying the amount. A petition will be drafted immediately and submitted to the province with the names and seals of those present, striving for the goal of verified collection, so as to meet the principle of equal burden.

Attempted Rape Foiled, Virtuous Woman Killed with a Knife: Zhang Rongsheng's wife, a farmer in Tinglin Liuyun Tu, was known for her virtue and seldom smiled or spoke. However, a rogue named Xue Qiaosheng had long harbored lustful thoughts towards her, but was always sternly rejected. On the 13th, Xue went to harass her again, but the woman remained resolute and rebuked him loudly. Enraged, Xue pulled out a sharp blade and stabbed her violently, causing blood to flow everywhere. After the attack, Xue fled and disappeared. The husband returned home and discovered the incident, immediately seeking medical help, but the woman succumbed to her injuries. Zhang Rongsheng was heartbroken and, after the funeral, reported the incident to the County Court Prosecutor's Office, requesting the arrest and punishment of the perpetrator to comfort the virtuous soul.

Suzhou 17

New Trends in Opium Monopoly: Due to opposition from various parties, the opium monopoly issue has undergone changes, transforming into a public transportation and sale of domestic opium, implementing a system of government opium and private sales. The Suzhou contractor is a Mr. Qiu, with 35 sub-distribution directors managed by Du Changlin and others. The Suzhou Anti-Drug Association has learned that the contractors are currently buying public opinion, providing monthly subsidies to newspapers: fifty yuan for broadsheets and thirty yuan for four-page and tri-weekly publications, for a period of three months, with payment due on the 20th. Negotiations for selling domestic opium are taking place at the Guo family's opium warehouse in Shanmen Lane, with the condition that the newspapers refuse to publish news from the Anti-Drug Association. Therefore, the association plans to issue a second declaration, firmly opposing the practice.

High Court Executes Murderer by Hanging: Gu Zengbao, a resident of Zhouzhuang in Wu County, was convicted of murdering Sun Baofeng, the husband of Sun Dan, a fellow villager, on July 8th of the 15th year of the Republic. After being apprehended, he was sentenced to death by the Wu County District Court. The third and final trial upheld the death sentence. With the approval of the Provincial Government obtained through the High Court, the prisoner Gu Zengbao was transferred from the detention center to the execution ground on the morning of the 17th at 8 AM and executed by hanging.

Wuxi 18

Misfortunes Befall Liu Laofu and Son: Liu Laofu and his son, Liu Rongsheng, residents of Shilangzhong Lane inside the South Gate, are both heavily addicted to opium. On the 28th of last month, they were suddenly arrested by the First Public Security Bureau and sent to the County Court Prosecutor's Office. After questioning by Chief Prosecutor Zhou, they were ordered to each pay fifty yuan in cash as bail. However, the Liu family was destitute and had to remain in jail. After Liu Laofu was imprisoned, only his wife, daughter-in-law, and grandson remained at home. His wife, Mrs. Yang, recently fell ill and was bedridden, moaning in pain. As if misfortunes never come singly, on the evening of the Mid-Autumn Festival, Liu's daughter-in-law saw bedbugs on her mother-in-law's mosquito net and used a kerosene lamp to catch them. By accident, the net caught fire. In an instant, the fire spread, and Mrs. Liu Yang was unable to escape, perishing in the flames. Liu's daughter-in-law also burned her right hand. Nearby neighbors rushed to extinguish the fire, finally putting it out. Afterwards, the Tu Zheng (local head) Wang Yongtai reported the incident to the County Court, requesting the release of either Liu Laofu or his son on bail in order to provide a coffin and bury the body. It is truly a tragic tale.

School Cook Poisons Porridge Pot: The County Girls' Middle School in Xiaolou Lane in the city has been established for many years and is thriving. In June of this year, Principal Gu Gujia, through Zhou Xieqing's recommendation, hired Hua Quan'gen as the food service manager. After three months, during the autumn festival, the school's general affairs officer, Guo Zhengmo, discovered that Quan'gen had embezzled all three hundred yuan of the school's food expenses, and that the rice, oil, vegetables, etc., were all purchased on credit. Furthermore, Quan'gen's cooking was unhygienic, so he was dismissed and replaced by Xu Alin. Resentful of his dismissal, Quan'gen plotted revenge. Yesterday morning, while Xu Alin was cooking porridge, Quan'gen secretly ordered his wife, Hua Jiang, and Zhu Rongchun to put poison in the porridge, causing the white porridge to turn a sauce-yellow color. The entire school, teachers and students alike, were in uproar upon seeing this, but fortunately, none of them had eaten it. Hua Quan'gen, Jiang, Zhu Rongchun, as well as Guo Zhengmo and Xu Alin, were all sent to the First Public Security Bureau. After a preliminary interrogation by Chief Gao, they were all sent to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation, along with the four barrels of poisoned porridge.

Silk Factories Continue to Request Rent Reduction: Due to the decline of the silk market and the failure of various factories, the silk factories in the county, led by Miao Shaoqing and others, jointly petitioned the County Government during this national crisis for a reduction or exemption of factory rent to ease their burdens. After receiving the petition, the County Government, citing the contractual relationship between the factories and the landowners, invited both parties to negotiate, but no concrete solution was reached. Yesterday, Miao Shaoqing and others continued their previous proposal, requesting the County Government to promptly convene the Party Department, the Chamber of Commerce, and factory owners and tenants to discuss and resolve the issue, in order to help Suzhou merchants in their difficulties.

Changzhou 19

Detective Team Captures Robbers: The Liu Sandajia family in Nanliujia Village, Heliu Township, in the Seventh District of Wu County, was robbed some time ago. Recently, the detective team captured Yin Heer, a robber involved in the case, who confessed to the robbery. Yesterday (the 16th), another accomplice, Yu Xida, was arrested and handed over to the county. After interrogation, Yin Heer confessed that Yu Xida had invited him to participate in the robbery, along with more than ten others, armed with six guns. He also said that the loot was distributed at Yu's house. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be shackled and imprisoned separately.

Carpenters' Guild Strikes: The carpenters' guild in Wu County went on strike on the 16th due to the unresolved issue of the "tie-ba" fee (a type of commission). They have stopped accepting measurements of timber rafts anchored above the Xinzha Dam and have secretly agreed that they will not work until the "tie-ba" fee issue is resolved. Violators will be punished as a warning. The timber merchants have not yet made any statement.

Special Issue on Aviation Construction

Compiled by the China Aviation Construction Association

The Establishment and Current Status of the China Aviation Construction Association 20

By Luo Yinpu

(I) Reasons for its Emergence: The China Aviation Construction Association is a direct product of the Shanghai War and a new expression of the Chinese people's awakening, gathering their practical strength to engage in aviation construction. During the Battle of Shanghai, the enemy, taking advantage of our weak air defenses, was able to maximize the power of their aircraft, causing immense harm to both our military and civilians. After the Shanghai War, the enemy was deeply impressed by the power of their aircraft and thus mobilized the full strength of their government and people to expand their air force. We, the Chinese people, being the victims, have learned a deeper and more profound lesson than the enemy. Therefore, after the war, the call for aviation to save the nation spread throughout the country. Overseas Chinese, in particular, actively promoted this cause, donating large sums of money or purchasing aircraft to assist the government in external self-defense. At this point, the Chinese people deeply realized that national defense is essential for saving the nation, developing aviation is essential for strengthening national defense, and developing aviation requires the combined efforts of the entire nation, assisting the government, and working together. Therefore, the organization of this association is a crystallization of this widespread sentiment.

(II) Process of Establishment: After the Shanghai War, in the wake of the severe pain, the Chinese people began to contemplate remedial measures. Realizing the weakness of our national air defense and understanding the limitations of the government's capabilities, they resolved to catch up, relying on the people. However, the people's strength was dispersed and unorganized, so without organization, the strength would be insufficient, and without unity, the results would be insignificant. Therefore, establishing an organization to promote and guide was essential. In April, Mr. Zhu Ziqiao, Mr. Xiong Xiling, Mr. Xu Shiying, Mr. Chen Lianbo, Mr. Lin Kanghou, Mr. Yin Zhiling, and other leaders from various sectors of society, together with aviator Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan, jointly initiated this association. Immediately, various sectors responded enthusiastically and agreed. On June 28th, the inaugural meeting was held at the YMCA in Ba Xianqiao, Shanghai. Over a hundred people, including the association's founders and representatives from various sectors, gathered to support this great cause, which was truly a grand event. With the foundation of the association established, the headquarters were set up at No. 610 Continental Mansion on Nanjing Road, and the application for registration was submitted to the Ministry of Transportation of the National Government, which was approved. The future success depends on the extent of our efforts.

(III) Objectives: What are the objectives of this association? In short, it is to realize the meaning of "aviation to save the nation." Everything from promoting the importance of aviation, training aviation personnel, developing the aviation industry, and establishing aviation factories are all activities that the association plans to undertake and strive for, all with the ultimate goal of saving the nation and strengthening the country. Today, the national crisis is at its peak, and the emptiness of our national defense is the reason for the humiliation. If we want to talk about national defense, there is nothing better than building a strong air force. To build an air force, it is essential that our compatriots across the country awaken, rise up, and contribute their human and material resources for national use, and ultimately achieve success. Building an air force is easy and quick, and its combat power surpasses that of the army and navy. What other path is there to self-strengthening? The association's lofty goals are well-founded. (IV) Current Situation: Since its establishment, the association has spared no effort in carrying out various tasks. We believe that although the people understand the importance of aviation, they have not made a firm determination to build it. Although society pays attention to aviation news, they have not deeply felt the interest in participating in learning. To promote and awaken, publicity is still needed. Looking around the country, the aviation community lacks both common publications and systematic works. Therefore, the association publishes special issues to promote aviation and compile series of books to broaden research. In addition, we organize publicity meetings, hold exhibitions, etc., to generate interest. This is the initial stage of the association's work. Today, the most difficult problem in China's aviation community is the lack of talent. Manufacturing requires talent, and piloting requires talent. Without talent, things cannot be put to good use. Therefore, education is still needed. In this regard, the association is preparing to establish aviation engineering classes to cultivate manufacturing talent and preparing to open aviation schools to train piloting talent (see the draft plan for the association's preliminary education and manufacturing work). Although the scale is small, the achievements are promising. Other important tasks are also being implemented in order. It is hoped that compatriots across the country will act with the sincerity of saving the nation and encourage each other.

(V) Welcome Compatriots to Join the Association: The association was born in the midst of national crisis and stands for the goal of saving the nation. Therefore, all compatriots have the obligation to participate in the work, either by participating in person or by providing financial assistance, each contributing their abilities and resources to help the development of the association. Then, in the future, our country will become an aviation country, our people will become an aviation nation, bringing light to the world and happiness to mankind. Is this not a dream? Is this not a dream?

Declaration of the Association for Soliciting Members 21

Since the loss of the Northeast, the people have been tormented by激昂and悲愤, and the government has struggled in a state of徬徨and无措. Time has passed, and the first year of that tragic and shameful event has already passed. The lost land remains, and the disasters deepen. Today, we are逼于生死存亡無可假借之機. If our people do not want to be slaves of a self-destroyed country, and do not want to be slaves of world shame, then we must urgently seek self-salvation. It is now 逼于千鈞一髮無可敷衍之候. In the Shanghai War, the defeat was not due to the army, nor to the battleships, but solely to the lack of air defense. The Northeast Volunteer Army, wandering and displaced, was not困于敵兵, nor吓于敵砲, but solely為敵機所摧殘壓迫. After the hard battle, Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan發為"空軍之威力, 施之於無抵抗之對方, 其效為不可思議,"之嘆息. Considering all these, we know that the欺壓摧殘suffered by our country and our people實在于空防之無備. Thinking of this, how can we not感痛. Our association was established after the Shanghai War,奮鬭於國難之中. Fortunately, we have received the enthusiastic support of our compatriots, and experts have worked hard to operate. The development of the association is逐日有增. Since the government approved the registration, the work has been even more active. Our colleagues do not feel菲薄and勉効涓埃. The 区区之望is在于集合全國民眾力量, 協助政府, 建設强大之空軍, 以自立于弱肉强呑之世界. This heart and this ambition, I think, is sympathized by my patriotic compatriots. Now, at the time of the tragic national disaster commemoration, we爰有擴大組織徵求會員之舉. When my compatriots see蒿目时艰and伤心国难, they should be able to群趋救亡之道, join this association, and共求中国航空之发展, and图自强于将来. Sincerely declare,伏维鉴察.

Wei Wo Linggui (Defend Our Territory) Inscribed by Cai Tingkai

This Association's Nationwide Telegram to Compatriots on the Anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation Incident: Work Together to Build Aviation 22

To all newspapers, all sectors, all institutions, all schools, all organizations, and overseas Chinese: Since暴日凭陵, the Northeast has fallen, the Shanghai War of Resistance has occurred, and our territory has finally been stained. Although it is said that the Japanese invaders are狂横and罔顧公理, the reason is that our 武備不修and國防虚弱, 實為啓侮诲禍之由. In the Shanghai War, our 19th Route Army奮力抗戰and屢挫兇頑, but in the end, due to the lack of resistance in the air, the soldiers lost the opportunity to歼敌. This is what Brigade Commander Weng, who guarded Wusong, painfully said. It is truly a浩歎. Today, General Ma Zhanshan is苦戰海倫, and is also facing oppression everywhere by enemy aircraft. There is no way to resist, the soldiers are displaced, which makes people悲憤欲絶. Comparing the past and the present, it is clear that without an air force, there is no way to win, and without an air force, there will be defeat. If one passes through the ruins of Zhabei and Wusong, and imagines the ashes of the cities in the Black provinces, can anyone not痛哭流涕? Since the沈變, almost a year has passed. The lost land has not been recovered, and the disasters are deepening. The bombing of Chaoyang has not stopped, and the enemy troops in Shanghai have increased again. The violence is不可逆覩. However, the way to self-salvation is在于人為. Our association is盱衡时艰and勉圖自效. We believe that saving the nation is 重於國防, and國防 is 首於空軍. The establishment of an air force depends on the共與其成 of our compatriots at home and abroad. Now, on the anniversary of the沈變, there should be a澈底救國建設空軍之議. I therefore offer four suggestions, and hope that you will consider them. (1) Local newspapers, magazines, and various publications should publish materials commemorating the national humiliation on September 18, with the focus on宣傳航空救國. (2) All sectors, all institutions, all schools, all organizations, and overseas Chinese should hold national humiliation commemoration meetings on September 18, with speeches or performances on航空救國 as the focus of commemorating the national humiliation. (3) The expenses for stopping entertainment and banquets on September 18 by all sectors, all institutions, all schools, all organizations, and overseas Chinese should be saved in banks or money shops to充航空建設基金. (4) From September 18, all sectors, all institutions, all schools, all organizations, and overseas Chinese should each pledge to建設航空, join this association, and共同努力 to固國防and紓國難. Alas, the national crisis has reached its peak. The機 of存亡 is繫於一髮. 載胥及溺, 能不凛然. Today, the Chinese people also know救國, and救國 must say aviation. The point is to見諸實行. The above four points, if we can achieve one, I hope that my patriotic compatriots will jointly plan it. I have always admired your熱忱and爱国, and I hope that you will inform your subordinates to implement it together. If you have any inquiries, please send a letter to the China Aviation Construction Association, Continental Mansion, Nanjing Road, Shanghai. The China Aviation Construction Association.
