Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau 54

Sends Chen Shunyun to Tianjin to Assist in Inspection Administration

The Tianjin Commodity Inspection Bureau mainly inspects livestock. In order to improve livestock inspection, the bureau has been approved by the Ministry of Industry to transfer Cheng Shaojiong, a technical officer from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, to serve as the Director of the Livestock Inspection Department of the Tianjin Commodity Inspection Bureau. Cai Wuji, Director of the Shanghai Bureau, obeyed the order of the Ministry but considered that Cheng Shaojiong's position in the bureau, overseeing the manufacture of foot-and-mouth disease serum, was important, and his departure might cause a standstill due to a lack of replacement. However, the Tianjin Bureau needed to improve livestock inspection urgently. To balance both sides, it was decided to send Chen Shunyun, Director of the Livestock Production Fermentation Department of the Shanghai Bureau, to Tianjin temporarily for three months to assist, and then return to the Shanghai Bureau after the term. Chen is scheduled to depart for Tianjin on the 20th to assist with all matters.

Qu County, Zhejiang 56

Sends Special Commissioner to Shanghai to Raise Relief Funds

The Exchange Association Generously Donates 1,000 Yuan

Qu County, Zhejiang, is located at the border of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Fujian. Since the insurgency of Fang and Shao bandits in eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian, refugees from various counties in eastern Jiangxi, such as Guangfeng, Shangrao, Guixi, and Yiyang, have flocked to Qu County, reaching several thousand. Initially, they still had some valuables to pawn, but recently they have been running out of resources. Those with several thousand dan of grain at home have been labeled as landlords by the Red Bandits and have been deprived of everything. Those with several sons who graduated from universities are now hiding in dilapidated temples, supported by their wives, concubines, and daughters begging for food. The wives, concubines, and daughters, accustomed to pampered lives, are ashamed to go out and often spend the entire day without getting a full meal. The county magistrate of Qu County, Wu Bokang, considering the hunger and cold of the refugees to be pitiable and recognizing that a failure to properly resettle them would inevitably lead to disturbances in local security, has specially requested Wang Hantao, the Ninth District County Administration Supervisor, to solicit donations from all parties. It is reported that Wang recently came to Shanghai and invited philanthropists and Jiangxi natives in Shanghai to a vegetarian meal at the Gongdelin Restaurant. Wang Yiting, Mu Ouchu, Zhao Jinqing, Qu Wenliu, Wang Rutang, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Huizeng, Zhang Shenzhi, Tao Xingru, Niu Yuanbo, Xu Hexuan, and others attended. Wang Yiting and Mu Ouchu, representing the Exchange Association, generously donated 1,000 yuan in silver. Zhao Jinqing also donated 100 yuan in silver on behalf of the China Sports Advancement Association, which was paid on the spot. The other philanthropists also promised to do their best to solicit donations, hoping that all sectors of society, mindful of the Red Bandits' ferocity and cruelty and the refugees' displacement, would enthusiastically contribute to save them from the floods.

Jiao Hu Gang Bandits Arrested and Transferred to Kunshan 57

Nie Shuqing, Xi Huazhai, Chen Yunting, Chen Yongqing, and other bandits from the Jiao Hu Gang in Anhui, who had previously committed a serious kidnapping case in Kunshan, were hiding in a thatched shed in Yidaikou, Zhabei. The Kunshan County Public Security Bureau sent detectives to Shanghai to investigate and learned of the bandits' hiding place. They reported to the relevant section of the Fourth District, who, together with detectives, went to Yidaikou and arrested Nie and the other four bandits. Two pistols and twenty-three bullets were confiscated on the spot. They were taken to the section of the Fourth District and reported to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. Qin, the Director of the Kunshan County Public Security Bureau, prepared a document and sent Yu Lin of the Detective Team to Shanghai to request the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to transfer them. Upon approval, Nie and the other four bandits, as well as the pistols and bullets, were handed over to the team leader and escorted to Kunshan by the Shanghai-Nanjing Express Train to be investigated and prosecuted.

Ma Dunhe Hat Shop Moves Back to New Premises 58

Ma Dunhe Hat Shop in Shanghai is recognized as the leading hat shop in the country. Due to the renovation of the building, it had temporarily moved to the opposite side of the street. Now that the original site has been completed, it has moved back to the corner of Er Ma Road and Wangping Street, i.e., the shopfront of the Continental Mansion, and is operating as usual. The decoration is brand new and magnificent. It is reported that the second and third factories of the shop, located in Zhabei, suffered severe damage during the Japanese invasion of Shanghai, resulting in significant losses. They have now been re-established one after another. The raw materials used are carefully selected from the highest quality goods, and the workers are all highly skilled. Therefore, the products are of excellent quality and novel in style. The shop also sells domestic ceremonial hats and European and American high-quality felt hats, caps, and children's hats, all of which are available. In addition, a hat cleaning department has been added, specializing in cleaning old Chinese and Western straw and felt hats using the small Luzon method.

Yang Laowu and Wife 59

Detained for Abusing Their Niece

Beating Her All Over and Depriving Her of Sleep

Neighbors Nearby Frequently Heard Her Crying

Yang Laowu, a native of Tongzhou, and his wife, Yang Tan, who reside at No. 767 Rongshou Lane, Avenue Edouard VII, are very cruel and abuse their eleven-year-old niece, Tan Lindi, all day long, causing her to be covered in wounds and depriving her of sleep, making her sit up all night. Neighbors in the vicinity frequently hear the girl's cries. A few days ago, Chinese detectives Zheng Huaili and Chen Dabao of the French Concession Police learned of this and secretly investigated, confirming the facts. Considering Yang and his wife to be inhumane, they arrested them and took them to the police station for detention. The girl, Tan Lindi, was sent to Kwang Jen Hospital on Avenue Albert for treatment. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Summary Court of the First Special District. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated the case, saying that the girl, Tan Lindi, was still being treated at the hospital and could not appear in court today, requesting a postponement for further interrogation. The defendants claimed that the girl was of bad character and often stole things, so they had slightly disciplined her. After reviewing the statements, Judge Liu instructed that the two defendants be detained for a further hearing next Wednesday.

Opium Hidden in Broom Handles 60

356 Ounces of Opium Seized

Seven Months Imprisonment and 50 Yuan Fine

On September 8th at 10:50 AM, Hu Dewang, a native of Henan, hired rickshaw No. 949 at the Jianghai Customs Wharf on the Bund, Fuzhou Road, to carry 41 brooms to Avenue Foch, French Concession. Chief Inspector Wu Chunrong and Chinese constables No. 766 and No. 1480 of the General Inspectorate saw that his actions were suspicious and intercepted Hu. They found 356 ounces of opium hidden in the broom handles. They were taken to the police station and handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide of the Criminal Court interrogated Hu Dewang. Hu Dewang insisted that two men in Zhongshan suits had entrusted him to carry them. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi, based on various circumstances, determined that Hu was the principal offender in the opium trafficking and requested that he be severely punished in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Opium Law. After deliberation, Judge Feng sentenced Hu Dewang to seven months of imprisonment and a fine of 50 yuan for assisting others in attempting to sell and possessing opium. The number of days of detention before the final judgment will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The opium and brooms were confiscated.

Two Young Men Attempt Suicide by Drowning 61

Fortunately, Both Were Rescued

Yesterday morning, two men, coincidentally, boarded ships at the Xinguang Pier one after another and attempted to drown themselves in the river. Both were due to economic hardship. Fortunately, they were rescued and did not drown. The details are as follows:

No Face to Live: Xiao Xinyuan, a native of Hunan, 30 years old, used to run a hotel in Shanghai. Due to poor business, he lost money and closed down. He has been unemployed for several years. This year, he suddenly suffered from pain in both feet. After borrowing more than 20 yuan from his uncle, he finally sought medical treatment and cured his foot pain. The other day, a friend invited him to seek work in Pinghu. Xiao, feeling ashamed to go to Pinghu because his clothes were old and worn, became ashamed and angry. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, he took the No. 11 ferry from Xinguang Pier to the other side of the river. When the ship reached the center of the river, he jumped into the water to end his life. The boatman, Fan Jinlong, immediately took measures to rescue him and sent him to the Customs Water Police Station. He confessed his situation and said that his uncle's name was Deng Youqing and that he worked at the Wanyuan Xiang Embroidery Shop in Huajin Lane, Hankou Road, and that his mother, Deng, also lived there. The police station dispatched Chinese detective Ge Changsheng to summon his mother, Xiao Deng, to the police station to take her son home.

Lacking Funds to Return Home: Shao Qiuzi, a native of Yongjia, Zhejiang, 24 years old, is a tailor. He used to work in a shop in Nanjing, but recently he stopped working due to some reason. On the 12th of this month, he took a train to Shanghai to find friends. After several days, he had not found them. His money ran out, and all his belongings were pawned. Seeing that he was at his wit's end, he wanted to return home, but he did not have a penny. He became weary of the world. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, he also went to the Xinguang Pier and boarded a ferry to the other side of the river. When the ship reached the center of the river, he jumped into the water to end his life. Fortunately, the crew rescued him and sent him to the Water Police Station. Seeing that his situation was pitiful, the police station dispatched Chinese detective Ge Changsheng to send him to the Wenzhou Native Place Association to find a way to send him back home.

Cai Xiqing Dies After Mistakenly Eating Poisonous Substance 62

Cai Xiqing, 31 years old, a native of Jiangsu residing at No. 25 Yili Street, Penglai Market, Penglai Road, Nanshi, worked for a foreign company. A few days ago (the 16th), he celebrated the Mid-Autumn Festival at home, inviting relatives and friends to a feast. He was in high spirits. After three rounds of drinks, Cai, as the host, initiated a drinking game. However, Cai's alcohol tolerance was not high. After drinking a few glasses, he became intoxicated. Before long, he vomited non-stop. His family helped him to the inner room to rest. After the guests finished their meals, they played mahjong. At 4:00 or 5:00 PM, Cai's drunkenness not only did not subside but also became accompanied by groaning and abdominal pain. At first, they suspected that he had cholera and treated him with Huoxiang Zhengqi liquid and other medicines, but it was ineffective. They then took him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was to no avail. He died yesterday. According to the doctor, it was feared that he had mistakenly ingested a poisonous substance.

Motor Vehicle Kills a Person 63

Judge: Car Owner Should Provide Compensation Quickly

Lv Aqiao, one of the two drivers of a truck owned by the Hulisheng Coal Company on Jiaxing Road, drove truck No. 18361 on the 10th of this month at 8:45 AM on East Seward Road near the No. 7 tram stop near Huaji Road. The driver accidentally knocked down Yi Jishan, 30 years old, a fellow villager who worked for a customs broker and resided at No. 3224 Puan Lane, Zhoujiazui Road. He was sent to Tongren Hospital by Chinese detective Zhao Ruisheng, but he died of his injuries at about 10:00 AM the next morning. Lv Aqiao was taken to the First Special District Court by the Wayside Police Station. Lv claimed that there was a collapsed car obstructing the road at the time, causing him to knock down the deceased. He was detained for questioning. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong opened the Criminal Court No. 4 for the trial. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that the investigation revealed that the defendant had taken the wrong route at the time, causing the accident. He asked that he be prosecuted. Qin Rongjun, a Korean tram ticket inspector on the No. 7 tram, testified that he saw the defendant's car not following the route. Liu Yao, the wife of the deceased, testified that her husband worked at a customs broker with a monthly salary of more than 20 yuan, leaving behind an eight-year-old son and that she was several months pregnant. At that time, her husband had left home to go to the office and suffered this misfortune. The owner of the coal company, the defendant, had asked someone to mediate and was willing to provide compensation of 1,250 yuan, but it had not been received yet. Chen Xinren, the representative of the coal company, said that the amount had been agreed upon by the deceased's wife and the owner of the coal company, Hu Lisheng, and that it could be paid this afternoon. The court declared to him that the deceased's wife was now widowed and helpless, and that the amount should be enough to support her for the rest of her life. He urged the owner not to break his promise. Chen agreed. Judge Shen ordered the defense to begin the debate and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody. The sentencing date was set.

He now has a clinic on the upper floor of the Jiangnan Bank on Henan Road, where he sees patients every day. Recently, a patient named Liang Zuxin, who resides in Minhou Lane, Hartung Road, suffered from scrofula neck for a long time and had sought various treatments without success. After seeking treatment from Dr. Xiang, he received multiple ultraviolet light treatments and injections. Within a month, his illness disappeared. Dr. Xiang's medical skills are indeed profound.

News from Various Labor Unions 76

Leather Industry Union Yesterday, an interim board meeting was held, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The factory of Xiang Sheng discharged as many as eighteen workers without reason. Although the Municipal Party Headquarters sent personnel to mediate, there is still no concrete resolution to this day. How should this case be handled? It was resolved to submit it again to the Party and government authorities for investigation according to law and not stop until the goal of resuming work is achieved. (2) The factory of Xiang Sheng ordered the dismissed workers to sign papers. How should the union deal with this case? It was resolved to send a letter to the employer for negotiation and to submit the case to the Party and government authorities to order the factory to reinstate the dismissed workers in accordance with the law. (3) The factory of Zu Sheng did not pay wages. It was resolved to send a letter to the factory, ordering immediate payment, otherwise the factory will be fully responsible for any disputes that arise thereafter. (4) The dispute over the shutdown of the Jingyi Factory was resolved to wait for the mediation of the Social Bureau. There were many other motions, which are omitted.

Smoking and Tobacco Industry Workers' Union Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the nineteenth executive committee meeting was convened at the office at No. 371 Haichang Road. Chairman Xu Zhongyuan reported on the work situation. The following matters were discussed: (1) Previously, because the executive committee members Wang Jiading and Zhu Zonglin left Shanghai for other jobs, members Sun Hantao and Peng Zhongkang were moved to fill the vacancies, but the matter was not reported to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Bureau. Now that Zhu Zonglin has come to the meeting, how should this be handled? It was resolved that the executive committee members should be formally elected by the representatives' assembly, and those who have photos registered with the Social Bureau are considered formal members. Sun Hantao and Peng Zhongkang are not eligible to be committee members according to the law. (2) The former executive secretary Wei Bing caused trouble. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter to the legal counsel to handle the matter. (3) There is no funding, and the office is in distress. How should this be remedied? It was resolved to follow the previous resolution and ask Comrade Xu Zhongyuan to maintain the office. (4-5) Confidential. (6) Chen Kehong proposed to organize a cooperative society for people in the smoking and tobacco industry. It was resolved to pass the proposal. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Weather Report 77

The Xujiahui Observatory yesterday at 4:30 PM issued a weather forecast stating that the coastal areas of Shandong are cloudy, with wind of undetermined direction. The coastal areas here and the Yangtze River basin are overcast but gradually clearing, with fog or slight showers. The wind is from the northeast. There is a gentle cyclone in the East China Sea, caused by a low pressure system moving northeastward. The center of a hurricane in the China Sea was at noon within 60 miles of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 113 degrees east longitude, moving northwest-westward, with fierce winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 70.7 degrees, and the lowest was 65.8 degrees. The highest temperature on the same day last year was 77.7 degrees, and the lowest was 66.9 degrees.

Letter Received 78

Dear Editor, Having read in today's (16th) newspaper that the village of Wangjiajing in Jiaotong Road sent a representative, Hou Xuanqing, to petition the Railway Bureau, after investigation, this is absolutely not the case. The so-called "representing the villagers to petition" in the newspaper is obviously completely inconsistent with the facts at the time. Fearing that there may be ulterior motives, I am writing to request that you correct the record to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Ding Zhenheng, Secretary's Office, Jinghu and Huhangyong Railways, September 17th.

Important Education News

National Salvation Cannot Be Achieved by Empty Words - Letter from the Minister of Education to Students Across the Country 80

Commemorating September 18th

Nanjing, 17th - Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua released a letter to students across the country on September 17th for the September 18th commemoration. The writing is elegant, from the pen of an old scholar. It concluded that national salvation cannot be achieved by shouting and jumping around, but only by empty words.

Nanjing - Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua's original text of the letter to students across the country for the September 18th commemoration is as follows: Time flies. It has been a year since the Japanese invaders spied on the border and the Eastern Provinces were lost to foreign lands. The lives of the people are trapped in water and fire, suffering hardships. Those who have died from displacement and from the sword can be counted in the tens of thousands. On the banks of Songhu and in the territory of Nenjiang, the sky is dark and the rain is wet, and the new ghosts are full of resentment. Indeed, it is a strange humiliation for the country, and the hatred is so deep that it makes one gnash one's teeth. The Eastern Provinces, in ancient times, were the territories of You and Qing prefectures. The north was the old land of the Sushen clan. When the Zhou Dynasty had virtue, its tribute of withered arrows was recorded in the past annals and spread as a beautiful tale. Since then, establishments have been established as prefectures and counties, and no inch of land is not our soil, and no one is not our people. In terms of its original expansion, fertile forests, and the abundance of agriculture, planting sorghum and soybeans is superior to China. There are 234 mountains that produce gold, silver, copper, coal, and iron, and the mines are often placed like chess pieces. To describe it ornately, it is truly a land of plenty. But Japan despises historical facts, betrays public agreements, flaunts its military anger, is heedless of its deceitful arguments, and is acting out a play of serving Puyi overtly while covertly threatening treacherous parties to seize our land and slaughter our people. The way of trustworthiness and righteousness has reached its end. In the past, they bravely crossed the sea, revered the holy lamp, and turned toward the wind, changing their old surnames. Now, comparing the past to the present, the traces of rise and fall are tragically profound. A country that is strong can sustain itself over long distances, but a weak country cannot survive. To restore the old ways and reverse the disorder in the world, every person has a responsibility. Students, work hard. Now the national crisis is urgent, and the troubles from the enemy are deepening. The central hub of Jianghan is also the lair of the communist bandits. Coupled with years of disasters, the people and things are withering, and people have no desire to live. The morality of the people is weakening, and the spirit of the people is languishing. They do not strive to uplift themselves, follow old ways, are content with the present, and do not care about the future. Because of their shallowness, they are shameless and increasingly profit-driven, so there are those who smuggle goods for the enemy and serve in the puppet court. The arrival of foreign disasters is like summoning them. It is like a body that is weak and first fears the wind and cold, which then attack and become serious illnesses. The past path has been overturned, and the coming path is just beginning. What will you students do to make things right? Moreover, international affairs change every moment. In short, the idea of military reduction is still empty talk, and the talks of peace are mostly fantasies. A small boat floats on the sea, and if the waves are high and the steering is like a god, it may still fall. How much more so when the boat lacks the skill to navigate and the passengers harbor feelings of competing to cross the river. Speaking of disasters and defeats, one must always be mindful of being on thin ice. Students, observe the national situation externally and examine yourselves internally. The task is heavy, and the road is long. It is disheartening. All wisdom in governing the country depends on learning, and the ability to handle affairs must be based on good health. Those who are weak and have waning spirits are not enough to go far. Those whose learning is sparse and knowledge is limited are not enough to handle affairs. You should devote yourselves to physical education, pay attention to science, store up knowledge, and practice talent to serve the country. How can you remain curled up and remain safe as a broken tile for a long time? Spiritual unity is the teaching of Sun Yat-sen. Traveling together in the same carriage is the command of wise men of the past, which should be regarded as a model to follow without weariness. Being firm and working hard are all ways to cure the bad habits of indolence and weakening spirits. This is the priority for managing affairs. What I have said today are things that you students have often heard, but I am still serious about them, just to prevent forgetting and to provide a warning. Extravagant and overflowing talk, and words that are too high-sounding and impractical are useless and only serve to increase arrogance, which students should not take to heart. There are many ways to save the country. The key is that it cannot be done by shouting, jumping around, stomping one's feet, clapping one's hands, and making empty statements. As I speak, my heart is running to the three islands of Fusang (Japan). Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Education (Central News Agency telegram, 17th)

World Tour Group Arrives in Peiping 81

Arriving in Shanghai from Peiping via Beijing on the 19th

Returning to Europe by French Mail Ship on the 24th

The World Tour Group proposed by Switzerland at the closing session of the International Olympic Games, with a group of twelve members, led by the head of the group Xue Mite (DR. Schmitr) and the deputy head of the group Ma Ding (DR. MarTin), arrived in Peiping (Beijing) from Shenyang the day before yesterday (the 16th). They will tour Peiping for three days and are scheduled to take the Peiping-Pukou express train to Beijing at 5:10 PM on the 19th. They will arrive in Pukou at 8 AM on the 21st and cross the river to enter the city. They will visit famous scenic spots such as Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, Ming Tomb, Mochou Lake, and Xuanwu Lake, and will take the night express train to Shanghai that evening. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai at 8 AM on the 22nd and stay at the Cangzhou Hotel (tentative). In the afternoon, they will visit the City God Temple and the streets of the city, Xujiahui, and the Catholic Church. They will have a leisurely tour on the 23rd and leave Shanghai for Europe on the French mail ship (Athos) on the afternoon of the 24th. The tour itinerary after arriving in China is all arranged by the American Travel Agency. It is recorded as follows: Arrive in Peiping from Shenyang on September 16th and stay at the Beijing Hotel. On the 17th, visit the Temple of Heaven, Altar of Agriculture, Liulichang, Confucius Temple, and Yonghe Temple in the morning, and the Imperial City, Ancient Palace Museum, and Central Park in the afternoon. On the 18th, take a train to visit the Great Wall. On the morning of the 19th, visit the Summer Palace. In the afternoon, visit the Peiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce and then go to the Peiping-Pukou Station at 5:10 PM to take the express train to Beijing. On the 20th, travel on the Peiping-Pukou Railway. On the morning of the 21st, arrive in Pukou at 8 AM, cross the river to enter the city, and visit famous scenic spots such as Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, Ming Tomb, Mochou Lake, and Xuanwu Lake. They are also scheduled to take the night express train to Shanghai that evening. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai at 8 AM on the 22nd and stay at the Cangzhou Hotel (tentative). In the afternoon, they will visit the City God Temple and the streets of the city, Xujiahui, and the Catholic Church. They will have a leisurely tour on the 23rd and leave Shanghai for Europe on the French mail ship Athos on the afternoon of the 24th.

Local News

Commemorating "September 18th" 85

Municipal Education Bureau Issues Circular

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued a circular to all municipal and private schools in the city, stating, "Regarding the telegram received from the Ministry of Education the other day, the telegram received from the Executive Yuan states, in brief, the central government has decided that the following three things should be added regarding the September 18th anniversary: (1) The flag should be flown at half-mast for one day on that day. (2) Although that day is a Sunday holiday, all agencies should still work as usual, all schools should still hold classes as usual, and all factories should still operate as usual. (3) All central government agencies should hold commemorative gatherings on the morning of that day. You are hereby ordered to comply, etc., as ordered. In addition to issuing separate orders, this letter is to notify you to comply," etc. In addition to issuing separate notices, corresponding letters should be issued to comply with the above.

Wang Qizhang's Opinion on Fasting

Mr. Wang Qizhang, a famous doctor in this city, sent a letter to the China Vocational Education Society yesterday, stating that the affairs of the country are in turmoil, and disasters are imminent on all sides. The Northeast has been in hiding for a year, and the blood of heroic men is boiling. They are sharpening their swords and gnashing their teeth, and cannot wait any longer. However, internal affairs are not being handled well, and the walls are not being repaired. External cooperation cannot be achieved any day, which is considered the most painful thing by those in the know. I have recently read the newspapers and deeply admire the great act of the gentlemen who advocate fasting at noon on September 18th to express their grief. They say that the saved money will be used to help the victims in the Northeast to wash away the strange shame. It is truly good and beautiful. However, I humbly suggest that the meaning of this be expanded and that a method be determined so that a certain amount can be obtained quickly without being empty words. According to the household registration of Shanghai, it is roughly assumed to be 3 million. These 3 million citizens naturally need to eat and drink every day. Now that it has been proposed to fast at noon, assume that the most frugal cost of this meal for each person is 5 cents, then 150,000 yuan can be saved from one meal. Using this to help the Northeast will not be without a small contribution. However, in fact, it may not be entirely possible, because the citizens must at least need this amount for each meal, and this meal may not be able to be saved (physiologically speaking, occasionally saving one meal and replacing it with two or three bowls of light salt water will not harm the body, but this is difficult to say for the laboring class). Therefore, it is impossible to force everyone to contribute these 5 cents. However, I also think that the need of a single dish saved by a family with fine clothes and good food can exceed this by several times. Therefore, by shortening the long and replenishing the short, it is possible to take the 3 million citizens of Shanghai as a unit and each do their best to make up the 150,000 yuan, which should not be difficult. For example, my family has a total of five people, and the average share for each citizen is only 25 cents. However, I think that although I am not rich, I still have the ability to pay for 199 citizens who cannot afford it, which is 9 yuan and 95 cents. This shows that among the 3 million citizens, there are 1,000 people who are like me, better than me by several times, hundreds of times, ten thousand times, or even a million times better than me. There are countless more citizens, and I don't know how many citizens they can afford to pay for. I deeply hope that you gentlemen will take this idea a step further and notify all organizations, agencies, schools, families, and the public in this city to do their best to contribute to the number of people they can afford to pay for. Then small streams will become a river, which can be expected to be established immediately. There is even more heart to advise the whole country to steal and hope for great success, etc.

Shanghai University Holds National Crisis Meeting Shanghai Hujiang University teachers and students have been deeply indignant about the national crisis since September 18th. This year, they encountered the Shanghai Incident, and they are even more excited to engage in anti-Japanese and national salvation work after class, vowing to actively seek knowledge and strengthen their strength with the spirit of lying on firewood and tasting gall, and to carry out a sustained and long-term struggle. It is scheduled to hold a "September 18th" National Crisis Commemoration Meeting in the auditorium at 9:00 AM this Sunday, chaired by Dean Fan. Professor Jin will give a lecture, and all new and old students are required to attend. At the same time, it will continue to promote Japanese studies, text propaganda, and national goods introduction. It is said that the National Crisis Commemoration Meeting of the affiliated middle school will be chaired by Director Li and various teachers will be invited to speak.

Since the National Labor University was ordered to suspend operations, the custody of the school's property has been extremely important. Alumni of Zhongguo Public School Organize a Reopening Committee 87

Zhongguo Public School is an academic institution with a rich history. It has been established for 30 years. The school site is more than a thousand acres and is located near the Wusong coast. It is large in scale and has achieved great results. Unfortunately, it was completely destroyed by the violent Japanese artillery fire in the January 28th Incident. Therefore, the school board of directors recommended Mr. Xiong Kewu as the president of the school to maintain it. Mr. Xiong is also a member of the Central Committee and cannot take care of both, so he strongly declined the position, which resulted in the failure to open classes this semester and a de facto suspension. The alumni of the school could not bear the interruption of studies and the loss of education for the students at the school, so they held a meeting to discuss the reopening issue at Liangyuan a few days ago. Hundreds of people attended the meeting, and a reopening committee was immediately organized. Zeng Bangxi, Chen Chaolun, Lu Congtang, Zhou Jisheng, and Yao Zhaoli were elected to be responsible for the work. It is said that the work has now begun, and the office is temporarily located at the law office of Yao Zhaoli, Zhonghe Bank, Shanxi Road, Nanjing Road. It is also planned to ask the founder of the school, Wang Jingfang, the school board members Cai Yuanpei, Yu Youren, and Wang Yunwu, and the alumni Hu Shi, Yang Xingfo, Zhu Jingnong, and Liu Binglin to find ways to assist in order to achieve the goal of reopening the school.

Grand Occasion of Pang Xunqin's Art Exhibition 88

The young painter Pang Xunqin studied painting and music in France for five years. He returned to China last year and devoted himself to Chinese painting, traveling to famous mountains and rivers, writing paintings and poems with great ease. In the past year, he has accumulated a lot of works. Recently, he was encouraged by friends to hold a solo painting exhibition at the Chinese Academy of Arts and Sciences on Aimaiyu Road from the 15th of this month for ten days, giving enthusiasts the opportunity to browse. Yesterday it was raining continuously, but the visitors were still very enthusiastic.

Olympic Miscellany 93

(Shen Siliang)

The Olympic Village: The organizing committee specially built the Olympic Village as a residence for athletes from various countries. The village consists of a total of five hundred houses, each with a central room, separated by a shower room and a balcony. The room is equipped with two exquisitely crafted beds, as well as straw mats and cane chairs. It is said that three thousand straw mats and five thousand cane chairs were custom-made in Hong Kong. The village has a theater where various dramas are performed every night for the entertainment of the athletes. Famous male and female movie stars from Hollywood have also performed there. There are post offices, wireless, and telegraph facilities. Each house is equipped with a telephone. The village is located on a hilltop, overlooking the entire city, offering a panoramic view. The grass is green, and the flowers are fresh, showcasing the beautiful scenery of nature. The village offers a variety of food, but some teams also bring their own cooks. It is said that the Japanese team brought their own ingredients. Languages from all over the world can be heard. The residents are very happy, as if they were in a paradise. Athletes can travel in and out of the village on dedicated buses, free of charge. After the closing of the games, the village will also disappear, as all the buildings in the village have been sold and will be used as seaside houses. Therefore, the organizing committee did not spend a penny to provide such a beautiful village for the athletes to live in, which is admirable.

The Assistance of Newspapers: The success of the games owes a great deal to the assistance of American newspapers. However, the organizing committee treats each newspaper equally and imposes strict restrictions. There is no possibility of increasing the number of seats for reporters. The reporters' seats are located in the highest row of the honorary seats, each equipped with a typewriter and a telegraph machine connected to the telegraph office. If reporters do not use a typewriter, they can directly use the telegraph or wireless radio to notify their newspaper. The competition among reporters from various newspapers is very intense. The telegraph office uses the latest equipment to transmit news quickly. Within five minutes after each competition, the newspapers have already received the news. In addition, wireless radio is used to broadcast news to countries around the world at any time. The relationship between the organizing committee and the newspapers is mutually beneficial and excellent, which China can learn from.

In this race, China scored six points, and Macleans scored three points.

(6) 200m Relay - The final event was the 200m relay. The talent on both sides was evenly matched, and the competition was very close. The difference was very small throughout, but the third Chinese swimmer entered the water too late, resulting in a defeat. Although Yin Yanjun tried hard to catch up in the end, he ultimately failed. The time was 2 minutes 13.4 seconds. Macleans scored four points. Macleans Team: (1) Huagen, (2) Burgess, (3) Shete, (4) Cole. Chinese Team: (1) Lin Jiangshui, (2) Zhang Yunqi, (3) Jiongde, (4) Yin Yanjun. The overall results are as follows:

Free Talk

Sayings of 93-Year-Old Ma Xiangbo: Words of Mourning for the September 18th Incident 95

The Northeast has been lost for a year, from September 18th last year to September 18th this year! The aggressors celebrate, while the invaded can only mourn. Old Man Xiang, at 93, has repeatedly expressed deep sorrow for this national humiliation!

I remember that on the eve of the national day of mourning for this incident last year, Old Man Xiang instructed me to write a message to the nation. After the draft was completed, because it was late at night, Old Man Xiang told me to send it to the Shenbao newspaper immediately. I took care of it in the dim night; but I caught a cold and got a cold; I thought that getting sick for the sake of the country was very proud. The next morning, I still took the text in the special column of Shenbao and sent it to Old Man Xiang to read in person. Some points were considered very correct, and some were considered inadequate. Later, he wrote a few paragraphs himself. I am now copying it out for use this year.

·······················

"The country is an organism. A country without national defense, and defense without secrets, is a country without land. If the four classes of people lack scientific knowledge (knowledge), and production, and the military and food are all taken from foreign goods, then there are no people. If politics does not follow administrative law (original note: Administration), then there is no government. Without government, there is no organism, and it is meat on the table, not a country."

"It is said: Cultivate yourself and do not blame others, then you will be spared from difficulties. It is also said: 'Defend the country and forget the dead.' Duke Wen of Wei wore clothes of coarse cloth and caps of coarse silk, devoted himself to materials and trained farmers, opened up trade and benefited craftsmen, respected education and encouraged learning, and assigned positions to the capable. In the first year, he had thirty chariots, and in the last year, he had three hundred chariots. If the people of the country can follow the morality and politics of Duke Wen of Wei, and save the money spent on opium and paper cigarettes in one year to build chariots, then it would not be difficult to have even three thousand, let alone three hundred! Or open a military factory to strengthen national defense. Why spend tens of millions of dollars every year to buy foreign weapons to kill compatriots, never being satisfied?"

"Alas! The whole country says that there is no conscience or religion! Since Xu Guangqi introduced Western water conservancy in Shanghai, and Wang Zheng wrote 'Wonderful Devices Explained' in Guanzhong more than three hundred years ago, the government has been unable to use domestic goods to build national defense, and the people have been unable to use science to create what they need for daily life. In the past fifty or sixty years, our eastern neighbor has been able to do everything that the western neighbor can do. It is appropriate for them to forget humanity and only think of Yi shooting for the sake of improving themselves! Being of the same culture and race is merely a saying for smiling tigers. How can it be believed?"

······························

Note: Last year, I included Old Man Xiang's mourning text in the "Collection of Mr. Ma Xiangbo's National Crisis Speeches" printed and distributed by the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association. You can write to the association to request a copy.

Silent Mourning 96

— Gao Qian

How Shall We Mourn?

September 18th has arrived. The bloody commemoration has reached its first anniversary! The National Government has ordered all party members and civil servants across the country to observe five minutes of silence at 11:00 AM to express their mourning. What are we mourning?

Dear readers, let us not sigh during these five minutes! Sighing shows weakness and incompetence! Let us not shed tears during these five minutes, tears show surrender! No! We want neither! We must strengthen our resolve during these five minutes!

What is the use of only blaming the government? Why do we not actively guide the government and cooperate with the government? Can selfish people like us produce an ideal government? Do not blame others, start with yourself! Students, workers, businessmen, think about how you can serve the country! How can you be worthy of the country? Let's all work hard! Starting from these five minutes, everyone should establish a way to serve the country, strive to do it, and not be too concerned about personal gains and losses. We must take the country as the premise. If the country is destroyed, we cannot be selfish. Government officials, I think you also have the same grief during these five minutes! But what is the use of mere grief? Let's not talk about the past. May you all not forget these five minutes. From now on, everyone should abandon personal interests and put the interests of the people and the country first, without failing the Party, without failing the country, and with one heart and one mind. Even if you cannot immediately eliminate the national crisis, you can at least be worthy of the Premier in heaven and the 400 million people below.

I Remember These Words 97

— Xi Niao

Deeply Engraved in My Heart, Never to Be Erased

"September 18th" jumps again in front of the Chinese people who are anesthetized by drugs. Early on, the calls for resolute resistance against aggression and determination to avenge...will be droning on people's ears again.

The newspapers are full of voices boycotting enemy goods, which truly chills the enemy's heart. In reality, which store can truly implement this in the midst of the storm of relying entirely on large-scale price reductions to survive?

The high-sounding call to promote domestic goods has now disappeared. Perhaps the period of promoting domestic goods has already become a thing of the past. Everyone! How many domestic goods have you bought?

Recently, I saw the words "Conscience Saves the Nation, Do Not Buy Enemy Goods" and "Those Who Give This Bill to the Enemy Are Thieves and Whores" written on banknotes. I don't hope for anything, I only hope that those who write those words are not just passionate friends who are just talking and writing.

I once heard a triumphant friend of the "Husband Serving Servant" theory say: "You men only know how to talk empty words, and there is actually no benefit at all. This is absolutely the opposite of the position that we women take in our actions, which is why we are successful." Ha! Men! Remember this! About all of this.

In elementary school, foreign goods are rarely seen in students' attire. In middle school, students' attire is a blend of Chinese and Western styles. In college, students' attire, perhaps due to reading too many foreign books, is like receiving a foreign education, with no trace of domestic goods to be found. Who says that the ability to save the country is transferred along with the level of knowledge?

September 18th and Bastard 98

— Bai Shi

China's National Humiliation Day is just like Wang Xiaoer's New Year, getting better and better every year. Look, the September 18th that no one ever paid attention to in the past has suddenly become a "September 18th" National Humiliation Day that is as fresh as can be this year.

The "September 18th" National Humiliation Day is today last year, when the Japanese, using the pretext that the South Manchuria Railway was damaged, sent troops to occupy the three northeastern provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang. Using underhanded means, they manipulated Pu Yi to create a puppet state, preparing to annex it in the future.

All previous National Humiliation Days were nothing more than opening concessions, recognizing indemnities, and signing humiliating treaties. This National Humiliation Day, however, gave an entire piece of land to others to use as a base, and a large number of people to be slaves. This shame is truly the ultimate shame.

I hope everyone will endure hardship and vow to avenge the national humiliation. Do not forget "September 18th" in a muddle-headed way. Forgetting "September 18th" is just being a "bastard."

Vanguards of National Destruction 99

— Zizai

May everyone pay attention!

The "September 18th" Incident is truly a national humiliation of unprecedented depth for our nation! Regarding this tragic national disaster that has awakened our minds and pierced our hearts, how should we endure hardship and encourage ourselves, be alert and awakened, and strive to be strong, so that we can unite as one, avenge our humiliation and save the country, and wash away the nickname of a sleeping lion!

Today is the painful commemoration of "September 18th." This shocking tragedy, no matter what, can never be forgotten! But alas, what kind of phenomena do we see around us today?

In theaters and playgrounds, there are still operas with urgent pipes and colorful costumes.

In restaurants, hotels, and brothels, it is still the same extravagance and debauchery with prostitutes.

In dance halls, it is still the same melodious music and revelry of lights and wine.

In cafes and massage parlors, it is still the same play and amusement.

In dog racing tracks and jai alai courts, it is still gambling with thousands of dollars.

In general clubs, associations, mansions, and shops, there is still mahjong playing.

In the park, there are still pairs of lovers holding hands, taking photos, talking about love, and coming and going.

How many of these people do not know the hatred of national destruction? If foreign enemies come, they will be the vanguards of national destruction. Let's all pay attention.

Rotary Club Silver Threads (17) 100

— Jiang Hongjiao

(9)

Fen Ruo suddenly walked to the window and stood there, thinking and considering, while tears fell silently on her lapel. She turned her back to Commander Yuan, her shoulders heaving.

"I should ask for your forgiveness. You have suffered all these hardships for the past ten years because of me. Now my pure and sincere soul is driving my body, teaching me to find you and ask you to discard all the sorrow in your heart. Let us hold hands and walk to the door of happiness again. Don't cry! You should remember the last time we separated. I hugged you like a provocation and said to you in a threatening manner: You said that one day I will come and disturb your heart, and hug you tightly so that you can't breathe after you get married. You replied to me: You are still so unprogressive, singing childish songs with a few children, and you won't sing marching songs. I have the strength to no longer give you any comfort or satisfaction. Fen Ruo! I have never forgotten this sentence that encouraged me. At any moment, or in any cubic inch of space, if you betray your previous words, I will tear up all my memories, tearing the curtain of my bright and happy hopes." Commander Yuan put his hands on her shoulders and turned his face towards Fen Ruo.

But Fen Ruo was still crying and shrugging her shoulders, especially heavily. Commander Yuan seemed to be at a loss for words, unable to think of any more real and touching words. So the room was silent for three minutes. Commander Yuan walked around the room, grabbing his head incessantly, feeling distressed and unable to solve the problem.

At this time, Fen Ruo suddenly turned around and went to Commander Yuan, saying, "Commander Yuan, please forgive me. I have considered it again and again. My previous behavior was so bad. I couldn't see through your true feelings for me. I have regretted it very much. Now I can no longer insult you with an unfortunate soul. This is my sincere intention. Please understand my circumstances. But I am unspeakably grateful for your sincere love. Please take care of your body, cherish your identity and reputation, and develop your future career! I now make a vow to sacrifice myself to find your abandoned wife. Although I have never seen what her face looks like or how tall she is, I imagine that her love for you has not waned. Suppose she is still alive and has not died. Please love her as much as you love me. You only need to think about the pain of your own heartbreak to imagine how your wife feels, and you will surely feel sorry for her and love her again. In these past ten years, I have become accustomed to a monotonous life. At most, I will spend another ten years or so, and then I will end my life's history. But your career is just beginning. Our country will never allow a hero to be mired in the trap of women's love again. If you really love me, you should understand these words of mine! My husband, although a soldier, his thinking and physique are really not worthy of being a soldier, although he has been dead for more than ten years, but I still have the right to criticize him, because he refused to listen to me and abandoned his indulgent life. Commander Yuan! I will always be a friend with you, and I will never throw away your figure and mind outside my brain, at any time."

Cotton Market Oppressed Heavily 107

American Cotton Has Fallen for Four Consecutive Days, and the Situation Is Still Weak. The People's Hearts in This Port Unanimously Watch the Fall, and The Large Households Exert Heavy Pressure. The Market Situation Is Still Shaking and Unstable. In the Early Market, Due to the Heavy Rain, the Cotton Is Currently Being Picked, Which Hinders Work. The Market Atmosphere Is a Little Tight. Stagnant Sales of Zhenmei Tea 116

The tea market in this port has been quite calm recently. Though there is still some sales of supporting teas like Zhenmei and Xiumei to France, the existing inventory is already running low. Most of the green tea available on the market consists of Zhenmei and Gongxi varieties. In particular, the Zhenmei teas from northwestern and northern parts of Wuyuan, despite being new, have only sold about one-tenth of their stock since their arrival in Shanghai. While there have been inquiries from Africa about the samples sent in recent weeks, the prices offered are considered too low. There has also been no progress with the teas from Tunxi, Shexian, and eastern Wuyuan regarding the Moroccan market. From the current situation, it seems that the prices of all types of red and green teas are likely to decline uniformly.

Sugar Market: Coarse Granulated White Sugar Rises Again by Five Cents 117

Yesterday, the sugar market saw good momentum due to the stability of the Dutch exchange rate. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's set prices also increased, with No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar priced at 14 taels, 5 mace, 7 fen, and 5 li, up five cents from the previous day. However, sales were limited, and the market expects further price increases. As today is Sunday, transactions are expected to be slow. The original Hong Kong ice flower green sugar was still priced at 12 taels and 2 mace yesterday, but merchants showed little interest, suggesting a possible easing of prices. Jianbing sugar, lacking supply, was not willing to compromise on prices, and sales were slow, resulting in no transactions.

North-South Goods: Chicken Heart Red Dates Saw New Arrivals Yesterday 118

The first batch of new chicken heart red dates, handled by Shen Hang's agent in Hankou, arrived yesterday. Due to the limited quantity, prices remained firm, selling for 11 taels. The inventory of Tianjin red dates has been dwindling recently, and prices have been stable. Yesterday, first-grade household red dates sold for 12 taels and 5 mace, second-grade household red dates for 10 taels and 5 mace, and third-grade household red dates for 9 taels. There were transactions both within this street and with the inland regions. It will be difficult for prices to ease before the arrival of new goods.

Hardware: Sales Show Activity 119

The continuous rain yesterday limited the number of industry peers in the market, and purchasing by out-of-town merchants was limited, resulting in scattered transactions. However, the Fujian merchants seem to be showing progress recently, purchasing more goods than other merchants. The key market conditions are summarized below:

Domestically Produced Small Wire Nails Sell Well Throughout the City: Domestically produced round nails (i.e., nails from local factories) have been widely sold both locally and in other cities, significantly impacting the sales of imported products. The newly released small wire nails, due to their low prices, have been selling quickly. Many local and out-of-town customers are happy to purchase them, resulting in considerable sales. However, recently, there has been a shortage of supply from factories, while demand is high, leading to occasional supply shortages. The prices remain strong, with 3-fen nails at 11 taels and 5 mace and 5 li, 4- and 5-fen nails at 11 taels and 3 mace and 5 li, and 6-fen nails at 10 taels and 9 mace. It is reported that the Fujian merchants have purchased 200-300 barrels in recent days, while the Yangtze River merchants have purchased 70-80 barrels.

10,000 Sheets of Domestically Produced Flat White Iron Sheet Were Ordered: 10,000 sheets of domestically produced flat white iron sheet, managed by the manager of China Steel Products Company, were ordered yesterday. It is reported that these were ordered by local merchants. Few out-of-town merchants have received this news, resulting in little transaction. First-grade products are priced at 8 mace and 8 fen per sheet, second-grade products at 8 mace and 5 fen, while thick patterned sheets had no transaction yesterday.

300-400 Tons of Bamboo Steel Bars Were Ordered: Yesterday, Fujian, Qingdao, and Yangtze River merchants purchased over 200 tons of bamboo steel bars, while local construction merchants purchased over 100 tons. In addition, smaller retailers purchased 70-80 tons. The price per ton is 65 taels, slightly up from the previous prices. It is said that the profit margins are thin, but market confidence is good, and the market anticipates further price increases.

Coal: Shanxi Coal Market Prices Gradually Loosen 120

Since the summer, the price of Shanxi white coal has been gradually declining, from 19 taels, 2 mace, and 5 fen per ton to 15 taels. However, despite the price drop, transactions have not improved, and the influx of goods from the mines has led to an oversupply in various warehouses, causing unstable prices. Yesterday, the market openly quoted a price difficult to call 15 taels, but slightly lowering it by 1 or 2 mace would make it possible to buy.

Commentary

From China's Current Education to Hosting Public Libraries (Continued) 121

— Wen Bing

The need for hosting public libraries has been discussed previously. Now, I will talk about the specific methods. In my opinion, we should not rely on the government for this kind of social undertaking, because facts have told us that anything that falls into the hands of our esteemed government will be messed up terribly. Therefore, for this kind of easy task, it is better for us, the people, to do it ourselves. Start with one or two interested and enthusiastic people to raise some funds (a hundred yuan is enough to start a library). To avoid spending on rent, it is best to set up the library in a private home and take turns managing it in the spare time of the morning and evening. Ordinary people who are under economic pressure and cannot afford to go to school but are busy with life can also take this opportunity to borrow books and read. Rules must be strict. The borrowing fee is one yuan, which is refunded at the end of the year, and paid again the following year. For each subsequent borrowing, a copper coin or two is charged. The interest from the deposit and the regular income from copper coins are used exclusively for purchasing books. With a clear conscience, public accounts should be kept to build trust in society.

Regarding the quality of books to be prepared, I feel that the city and countryside should not be the same. The reasons are: (1) the lifestyles of the city and countryside are different, (2) therefore, the needs and interests of the people in terms of books are also different. However, one should not be too extreme. One should strive to converge and integrate the lives of the city and countryside while adapting to each other's environment. In terms of level, the city should be slightly higher, with at least the level of a first-year junior high school student. The countryside should be slightly lower. The fundamental condition is that the writing should be in simple language, and the reasoning should be clear and concise so that readers can easily understand. Therefore, those who identify and prepare books should not only have deep knowledge but also carefully consider the needs of their community. One should not be perfunctory. Now, I will list the categories of books below.

For the public library in the city:

(1) Medical and health books: there are many urban residents, the air is polluted, and the society is complex, so this type of book is very important.

(2) Industrial and commercial series: to meet the needs of general store employees and workers.

(3) National ideology series: to import national ideology and resist the oppression of imperialism.

(4) Books that expose the dark secrets of the authorities: so that everyone can understand the pros and cons and not blindly follow, such as only focusing on civil war and not resisting imperialist aggression.

(5) Literary books: to cultivate morality and relieve

Page 23

spirit.

For the public library in the countryside:

(1) Books that break superstitions: Superstition is prevalent in the countryside, hindering social evolution, so more of these books should be prepared.

(2) Agricultural series: Various methods in Chinese agriculture are from thousands of years ago, and new knowledge should be imparted.

(34) (Same as the city's)

(5) Introductory industrial books: to improve general handicrafts.

(6) Farmer's literature books: Must be simple and stimulating, so that villagers can also receive some intellectual comfort.

With this method, as long as three or four people take the lead and achieve good results, it will not be difficult to spread to all parts of the country. I plan to host one when I return to my hometown at the end of the year. This is just my humble opinion, and I dare not say it is appropriate. I hope that all enthusiastic members will discuss it together.

Science

Several Kinds of Chemical Gold Plating 124

— Jiang Tianlan

A. Gold Plating on Iron Wire

Gold or silver plating on iron wire is very beautiful and easy to do. Simply soak the iron wire in dilute sulfuric acid, then place it in concentrated nitric acid to etch away the rust on the iron wire. However, a little smoke should be added to the nitric acid. After the iron rust is etched away, wash it with lime water, then rinse with clean water. Tie a piece of lead sheet to one end, then immerse it in copper water to plate a layer of copper. Then wash it with clean water. If you want to gold plate it, put it in gold water. If you want to silver plate it, put it in silver water. After plating, place it in hot sawdust to dry it quickly.

(1) Copper Water Recipe: 36 parts sodium hydroxide, 30 parts potassium tartrate, 7 parts copper sulfate, 200 parts rainwater.

(2) Gold Water Recipe: 10 parts gold chloride, 150 parts potassium cyanide, combine in 500 parts rainwater. Separately, 30 parts potassium hydroxide, 55 parts sodium hydroxide and phosphorus pentoxide, combine in 500 parts rainwater. Mix them together to form.

(3) Silver Water Recipe: 500 parts silver nitrate and dilute nitric acid, 350 parts potassium cyanide, 1000 parts rainwater.

B. Gold Plating on Copper Utensils

Whether it's yellow copper or red copper, gold plating is very simple. Dissolve 3 mace of real gold in aqua regia to make a kind of gold chloride, add 2 liters of distilled water, 1 pound of potassium hydroxide and potassium carbonate, and boil for 2 hours. Then wash the copper utensils and ornaments clean and immerse them in the liquid for a minute at most to create a golden and brilliant item.

C. Gold Plating on Glass

Gold-plated glass is indeed a valuable modern decoration. The method is very simple, just use three liquids: 20 parts of liquid A, 50 parts of liquid B, and 5 parts of liquid C, and mix them together. First wash the glass with alkali water, apply the liquid, and after a while the gold color will adhere to it. It will not peel off over time.

(1) Liquid A Recipe: 20 parts gold chloride, 150 parts distilled water.

(2) Liquid B Recipe: 50 parts anhydrous sodium hydroxide and light magnesium hydroxide, 20 parts distilled water.

(3) Liquid C Recipe: 20 parts alcohol, 20 parts pure acetaldehyde, 2.5 parts glucose, 30 parts distilled water.

Tumbler Doll 125

Society for Social Improvement Discussion

Discussion on Improving the Rental System 126

— Lu Fengzhao

In this city, most rentals are sub-rented from second landlords. To make a profit, second landlords modify the houses arbitrarily, harming public health and demanding rents at will, with no uniformity in prices. Measures should be taken to improve this to maintain the livelihood of ordinary people. "Reason" In Shanghai, apart from the general bourgeoisie who own their own houses or rent entire Western-style houses, the rest of the ordinary people mostly live together in a lane house with four or five families, with one family acting as the second landlord in charge.

The second landlord rents the entire house, and apart from their own needs, sub-rents the rest to other families. This was originally a cooperative nature, a good idea,

But the current second landlords (this refers to the general ones, not all second landlords in Shanghai) are becoming more and more sophisticated. They modify the houses arbitrarily, regardless of hygiene, as long as there are more rooms, they can rent out more rent. Therefore, these second landlords not only live in the houses for free, but also make money. They rely on being second landlords to maintain their lives, and they have a way to make money, which is admirable. However, because second landlords want to make money, they become third tenants, desperately increasing rents. For the same room, some second landlords only charge ten dollars, while others charge fifteen dollars. The third tenants, because they do not have the ability to be second landlords, reluctantly endure. When unexpected things happen in the inland, they take advantage of the fire and rob three times the profit, which is painful to say.

Among the members of this association, I assume there are both second landlords and third tenants, so I propose this issue for everyone to discuss. How can we stop these tricky second landlords? This is my only hope.

Attached opinions

(1) In my opinion, each neighborhood or block should have the landlord, based on the rental price of the entire building, plus land tax, water and electricity fees, and a portion reserved for vacant rooms, set a price that both second and third tenants must comply with. If they increase it arbitrarily, their qualifications as second landlords will be revoked.

(2) The police authorities should pay close attention to the modification of houses in the neighborhood or block to avoid affecting hygiene and public safety.

Please decide whether the above two items are appropriate.

Why

From "Leek Stir-Fry with Shredded Pork" to "Incense-Burning Old Lady" 127

— Yiyi Hall Owner

The day before yesterday, I went to a restaurant with four friends. One of my friends, Mr. A, liked to eat "leek stir-fry with shredded pork," so we ordered that dish.

At the same time, Mr. A suddenly asked a strange question: "People say that 'leek' is a meat dish, what's the reason?"

Mr. B continued, "Also, 'onion' and 'garlic' are also said to be meat dishes, I really don't know what the reason is?"

Mr. C, who likes to be funny, laughed and said, "Maybe Jesus has his own reasons."

Mr. D, who claimed to know, explained, "This is because of the smell. Because 'leek', 'onion', and 'garlic' all have a smelly taste."

Mr. A, who liked to eat "leek," thought that Mr. D's explanation was not sufficient, so he disagreed and said, "Then, why is 'stinky tofu' a vegetarian dish?"

Mr. C, who likes to be funny, said, "Really, if 'leek', 'onion', and 'garlic' are said to be meat dishes, then 'rice' and 'wheat' can also be said to be meat dishes. Wouldn't vegetarians starve to death?" Mr. B said, "Vegetarians are just deceiving people! Often some bad things are done by vegetarians!" Mr. D had just finished eating, and after hearing what Mr. B said, he put down his bowl and chopsticks and said, "This is called 'If you want to find a black-hearted person, look for them among vegetarians!'"

Seeing them saying one sentence each, I thought it was interesting, and after listening to the sentiments of Mr. B and Mr. D, I also joined the discussion and said:

"Probably these vegetarians are originally 'black-hearted people'? Because eating vegetarian food can reduce their sins, right? The strangest thing I find is this kind of 'incense-burning old lady.' When they go to the temple and meet their comrades, they always talk about the bad things their daughters-in-law do. They are always chanting Buddha's name while talking about how bad their daughters-in-law are. This is really absurd!"

When I got to this point, everyone had finished eating. Mr. A picked up a cup of tea, just about to kiss the cup, when he heard me talking about the evils of "incense-burning old ladies," so he put the cup of tea back and said, "Mr. Shen is right! In my hometown, there are two sayings, one is 'Speak ill of your daughter-in-law when entering the door, speak of oil tofu when leaving the door,' meaning that they speak ill of their daughters-in-law when they enter the temple door, and when they leave the temple door, they talk about how delicious the oil tofu in this temple is!"

After Mr. A finished speaking, the funny Mr. C chanted "Amitabha!" Everyone laughed when they heard it.

Shanghai First Special District Local Court 129

Public Notice Public notice of auction It is hereby announced that the court has confiscated the equipment and sundries in the case of Xu Shengquan's guarantee for absconding, and the valuation has been completed. The auction date is set for the 23rd of this month. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the bailiff to cooperate with the bailiffs to implement the auction. All residents who wish to purchase these properties should come to the bailiff's office of the court to report so that they can be led to the location to inspect them before bidding on schedule. If there are two or more bidders, the bidder with the highest price will be the buyer, and the auction items will be given to them for collection after paying the full price on the spot. All residents are hereby notified. Criminal Judgments:

Police Department v. Liu Wenxiang et al. for Using Counterfeit Currency (Verdict): Liu Wenxiang and Chen Ziqing are both not guilty. 131

Police Department v. Gao Xiaoyun et al. for Injury Resulting in Death (Verdict): Gao Xiaoyun is sentenced to eight years of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for eight years for the crime of joint injury resulting in death. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Xu Xiaosanzi (i.e., Xu Xiaotzi) is not guilty. 132

Police Department v. Lu Qilin et al. for Theft and Stolen Goods (Verdict): Lu Qilin (i.e., Lu Jili, also known as Lu Qilin) is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of burglary at night. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Wang Maoxi is fined thirty yuan for the crime of receiving stolen goods. If the fine is commuted to detention, it will be at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the fine at a rate of one day for every two yuan. Stolen foreign currency of twelve yuan, small foreign currency of six jiao, and thirty-one copper coins are confiscated. 133

Police Department v. Ji A'gen for Robbery (Verdict): Ji A'gen is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of robbery. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. 134

Police Department v. Yu A'jin for Robbery (Verdict): Yu A'jin is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of joint robbery. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. 135

Police Department v. Zhang Fengyuan et al. for Robbery (Verdict): Zhang Fengyuan (i.e., Zhang Fengyuan) and Wang A'qing (i.e., Wang A'qing) are each sentenced to three years of imprisonment for the crime of habitual robbery. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Zhang Fengyuan and Wang A'qing shall be jointly liable for compensating Zhou Ni's family for a gold bracelet. 136

Police Department v. Zhou A'si et al. for Opium Offenses (Verdict): Zhou A'si and Yan Lisheng are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Yan Lisheng is granted a three-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated as per the list. 137

Police Department v. Wang A'san et al. for Opium Offenses (Verdict): Wang A'san is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of providing a venue for others to smoke opium for profit. Xu A'gen and Li Baoquan are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Xu A'gen is granted a three-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated as per the list. 138

Police Department v. Zhao Liankui et al. for Opium Offenses (Verdict): Zhao Liankui is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan for the crime of providing a venue for others to smoke opium for profit. Wang He and Jin A'san are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. If the fine is commuted to detention, it will be at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Two opium pipes, one lamp, one needle, nine small boxes of opium, and half a can of opium paste (weighing eight liang in market weight) are confiscated. Wang He is granted a three-year suspended sentence. 139

Police Department v. Zhou Jinda et al. for Opium Offenses (Verdict): Zhou Jinda and Zhang Jinbiao (i.e., Zhang Jinbiao) are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Zhou Jinda and Zhang Jinbiao are granted a three-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia and opium bubbles are confiscated as per the list. 140

Police Department v. Shi A'gou et al. for Opium Offenses (Verdict): Shi A'gou is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of providing a venue for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. The number of days detained before the verdict is finalized shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment.
